worthy man incressit abandoun hart full mekill cair saw sutheroun multiplie mair mair self oft wald mak mane gude kyn yai slane mony ane yit semely stark bald age seuintene wynter ald wappinnis bair outher gude sword knyife thame hapnit richt oft stryife quhair fand ane ane vtheris presence efter scottis thay na mair offence cut throit stik suddandly waynit nocht fand yame anerly sindrie wantit yairto play ane hielie schrew wantoun intent wallace saw towart went lyklie richt big weill besene intill ane weid gudly ganand grene callit said thow scot abyde quha deuil quod graithit sa guid weid ane hors mantill war thy kynd weir ane scottis quhittill vnder thy belt beir rouch rillingis vpon thy harlotis feit gif thy knyfe quhat doi thy geir sa meit yeid knyfe tak fra fast collar wallace ta vnder hand knyfe braidit men yat semblit bot help self wist na remeid without reskew stikkit deid squyar fell yair na mair men followit wallace wounder sair preis thick cumerit yame full fast wallace spedy greitly al agast bludy knyfe drawin hand spairit nane befoir fand hous knew eme ludgit thidder fled farther micht nocht win gude wyfe thair within clois saw help cryit yat deit tre young capitane he fallin stryfe dur went gude wyfe ane russat gown hir awin scho gaif abone weid couerit laif ane suddillit courche ouir nek heid leit fall ane worne quhyte hat scho braissit yai suld nocht lang tary gaif ane rock syne sat doun spin sutheroun socht quhair wallace dreid thay wist weill quhat yet yeid hous thay socht besely bot sat still span richt cunandly tyme nocht leirit lang thay left sa furth gait gang heuy cheir sorrowfull thocht na wit yan get culd thay nocht inglismen barrat boun bad fyre scottis war toun yit gude wyfe held wallace vntill nicht maid gude cheir syne put sicht throw ane dirk gait scho gydit full fast couert went syne vp watter past forbure gait wachis thair mother ane greit despair quhen scho saw scho thankit heuinis king said deir sone sa lang quhair he declairis wallace slew churll awin staf air cap j young wallace yan fulfillit hie curage pryis armis desyrous vassalage thy vassalage may neuer forlorne thy deid knawin yocht ye warld sworne thy haill full oft refeit stuf hous full oft beit sa desyrit toun air se chyld na tuik ay nixt wod wallace gart leif hors syne suit yeid mercat cro peirse castell air inglismen greit number repair toun reulling yair awin wyse mony scot yai full greit suppryse abaissing wallace amang thame yeid rage youth maid haue na dreid ane churll thay yat felloun burdingis bair exceidingly wald lift mekill mair ony thre yat yai amang thame fand al ane sport tuik hand bure ane sting ane busteous poill braid bak ony wald thoill bot ane groit al fast micht draw quhen wallace hard speik mery saw desyrit mercat ane straik bad groitis thre churll grantit proffer fane pay siluer wallace full bane wallace sting tuik vp hand full sturdely befoir couth stand wallace vpon bak gaif quhill rig bane sunder draif carll deid speik na mair inglismen assemblit wallace thair feill feild folkis fecht fast vnabaisit nocht greitly agast vpon heid sting ane hit quhill bane brayne gart pecis fle ane vther straik ane basnet steill tre thair raif fruschit euerilk deill sting tynt inglisman deid craig bane brokin steid drew ane sword helpit neid throw thickest preis yeid hors full fane wald haue bene twa sairit maist yat cruell kene wallace returnit man mekill mane ane straik formest be slane ane felloun straik ye tother gat tyde gude sword gart thair abyde corslait brymlie bair groundin sword throw body schair fyue slew thair past fra toun gat hors laglane maid boun keipit chyld leit nocht abyde eschaipit thus laglane ryde feill followit hors al fute tak wallace na bute treis thick keipit full weill bot thair byde yat couth nocht adeill gude ordinance yat effeirit stait custume tyme baith air lait squyar wallace ouchterhous yat baith bed meit maid pa tyme remanit thair bot sair langit se toun air thidder past vpon ane mercat day wald god biddin away emis seruand fische send schir ranald craufurd yt schiref yan kend phow wallace slew lord peirseis stewart tane presonit air cap ij qvhen tane sic gude bocht peirseis stewart richt sadly socht said thow scot quhome byis thow thing ye schiref said heuinis king lord sall haue syne ga feche mair wallace cace neir gangand thair yeid said deir freind pray schireffis seruand yat yow wald lat ane lordly man stewart blude thocht wallace chargit termis rude ga hyne yow scot ye mekill deuill speid thy schireffis vse thow wenis v leid ane hunting staf hand bair thair smoit william wallace thair bot tre full lytill sonye maid fast collair claucht withoutti baid ane felloun knyif fast hart straik syne fra deid schot richt suddandlie catour sen syne trow na mair inglismen assemblit wallace thair four scoir war set armour burneist boun mercat day scottis keip toun wallace baldly drew ane sword weir birny formest couth beir throw body stikkit deid inglismen war bargane boun thay keip gait speiris rude lang dynt sword na man micht gang wallace harnest body weill thay socht schairp swordis steill fra strenth inueronit throw preis ane syde brak vnto ane well stude sey syde weill wo thair must neid abyde part yair speiris pecis thair schair fra ye castell vther help come mair ouir dyke yai glaid ather syde brak doun wall na succour tyde wallace wist na wane bot de wyn deid amang thame thus yeid vther part greit ire heuand fast byrneist brand brystit last brak hyltis away blaid flew wist na wane bot furth knyif drew first slew quhilk hand he hynt vther twa stikkit dynt remanent speiris he socht bure ground farther micht nocht lordis bad yai suld nocht sla pyne mair thay chargit ta thair innis suppois yat sworne gait force thay haue borne thus gude wallace inglismen tane falt help allane culd nocht ceis curage sa bair freuoll fortoun he brocht snair thir fals goddes full vnrichteousnes fals iuno full dowbilnes thay fenyeit goddes yit wallace neuer knew greit rychteousnes ay mercy drew kyn micht nocht get na kin thing micht thay haue payit ra soun ane king mair thay bad mair vane yair best men yat day seuin he slane thay sall thow rew sen power thus suddandly gane worthy scottis almichty god yow leid sen na mair worschip may yow speid presoun heir worthis mischeif sel e scotland help he greit neid thy natioun standis formit forsy fold pcomplene ye pure yus cedullis tellis complene heuin wordis nocht faillis complene voce greit god abuif complene sittis sytehfull cellis complene pane thus dollour dwellis langour iudgement quhair suld thoill law man went doun suddandly saw sicht deith snappit snell syne said thame he payit aw quhen thay presumit suld verray deid thay gart seruandis withouttin langer pleid schort auise vnto wall beir thay cais ouir bailfull steid thay trowit thair suld na remeid ane draf mydding quhair remanit thair first nureis new toun air scho come quhilk full reid purchest leif away body wesche quhill filth past hart wicht flikkerit fro twa ene last kest vp also foster mother luifit ouir laif gat mylk warme lyfe gif scho micht saif hir cure greit kyndnes couth kyith hir dochter heir thir termis rude better thinkis first hound micht greit stopping al faudoun haldin greit suspisioun knawin brukill complexioun richt stark bot lytill gane thus wallace wist bene left allane war fals enemeis wald ga gif war trew sutheroun wald sla micht ocht bot tyne fra questioun schortly pa deme ye list ye best may bot reheirs myne author say sternis began appeir inglismen wa cumand wounder neir fyue hundreth haill war cheualry nixt strenth wallace hy steuin ireland vnwittand wallace gude keirlie baid still neir hand place mure syde ane scrogy slaid eist duplin quhair thay tary maid faudoun left besyde thame land power come suddanly fand thair sluith hound graith way yeid vther tred scho tuik na heid sluith stoppit faudoun still scho stude na forther wald fra tyme scho fand blude inglismen demit vther yai couth tell bot yat ye scottis fochtin amang yame sell richt wa thay war loissit thair sent wallace twa men amang oist went dissimulit weill na man suld thame ken richt affeir thay war inglismen keirlie beheld vnto bauld heroun vpon faudoun luikand doun ane subtill straik vpwart tuik tyde vnder cloik grundin sword glyde gude mai ye baith craig hals bane sunder straik thus endit chiftane ground fell feill folk thrang tressoun thay cryit ane tratour v amang keirly slaid ane syde fellow steuin thocht na tyme byde fray greit fast away thay yeid baith toward erne thus chaipit yai dreid butellar wa weiping micht nocht stynt thus reklesly gude knycht haue thay tynt thay demit wallace men elli self thocht thay culd nocht ken richt neir sall haue aill f ill wod may lytill auaill fourtie thair past agane sanct iohnstoun deid corp burying maid boun partit thair men diuers wayis raid ane greit power duplin still thair baid danrich butellar past let sundrie furdis gaitis vmbeset keip wod quhill day thay thocht wallace thus thick forest socht twa men mynde greit pane wist nocht weill gif thay war tane slane chaipit haill ony iepardie threttene war left na gask hall thair ludgeing haue thay tane fyre gat thay sone bot meit thay nane twa scheip thay tuik besyde thame ane fald ordanit supper semely hald graithit haist sum meit thame dicht sa hard thay blaw rude hornis vpon hicht twa send furth luik quhat micht thay baid richt lang na tythingis hard bot busteous noyis sa brymlie blawand fast sa vther twa wod furth past nane come agane bot busteously blaw greit ire fend thame furth raw quhen allane wallace left thair awfull blast aboundit mekill mair trowit weill thay ludging sene sword drew nobill mettell kene syne furth went quhair yat hard ye horne without dur faudoun beforne sicht heid hand ane croce maid quhen sa saw stand wallace heid swakit thair haist sone hynt hair syne agane couth cast hart greitly agast richt weill trowit na spirit man sum deuill sic malice began wist nane auaill thair langer abyde vp throw hall thus wicht wallace glyde ane clois stair burdis raif twin fyftene fute large lap furth vp watter suddanly fair agane blent quhat apperance saw thair thocht saw faudoun vgly syre vpon hous laif fyre ane greit rufe tre hand wallace na langer wald stand gude men full greit meruell thay war tynt throw fell fantasie traistis richt weill suith deid supppois na point creid power thay lucifer fell tyme departit fra heuin hell sic mischeif gif men micht loist drownit slane amang inglis oist quhat lyknes faudoun quhilk brocht men suddand confusioun gif man endit euill intent sum wickit spirit agane present speik sic diuinitie clerkis wil lat sic mater bot wallace furth yow tell quhen went perrell fell yit glaid chaipit sa bot men greit murning flait self maker abufe quhy sufferit suld sic panis prufe wist nocht weill gif goddis richt wrang fortoun fulfill pleisit god trowit micht nocht suld set sic perplexitie bot greit curage mynd euer draif inglismen ane mendis think haif thus walkand allane vpon erne syde makand ane pieteous mane schir iohne butellar wache yai furdis richt fra men wallace ane sicht myst went mountanis gane raid quhair maid mane loud speirit quhat art thow walk yi gait ane trew man schir thocht vayage lait erandis pa fra vnto lord schir iohne stewart ye richt quha wil record new cumin fra king butellar said ane selcouth thing thow leid said thow he bene wallace sall knaw thow cum place stert cursour wounder wicht drew sword syne maid licht abone kne gude wallace he tane throw thee braune suder straik bane derfly ground knicht fell land wallace hors sone sesit hand ane akwart straik syne tuke steid craig twa butellar deid ane inglisman saw thair chiftane slane ane speir reist kest mane wallace draif fra hors beir warly wrocht worthie man weir speir wan withouttin mair abaid hors lap throw ane greit rout raid dalrich knew fuird full weill befoir come feill stuffit lyne steill straik first baid blasoun quhill hors man flet watter doun ane vther sone downe fra hors bair strampit ground drownit without mair thrid hit harnes steill throw coist speir brak ilk deill greit power efter ryde saw na wisdome thair langer abyde burnist brand hand braithly bair quhome hi richt thay followit na mair uf chace freikis followit fast bot wallace maid gayest ay agast mure tuke throw thair power yeid hors gude bor yit greit dreid failyeing wan strenth chace greit scaillit breid lenth throw strang danger thay ay sicht blak furd thair wallace licht hors stiffit way deip lang ane large lang myle wichtly ute gang horsit rydaris kest saw full weill lang sa micht nocht lest sad men deid vpon renew without recouering twentie yat nicht slew feirsest ay rudely rebutit keipit hors rycht wisely fle quhill come mirkest mure amang hors gai ouir wald na farther gang wallace fute tuke gude intent hors slew farther went inglismen suld haue na gude left fute weill vnderstude sutheroun men suld haue na sicht heich hadder past micht throw dark mure fra yame yan he socht bot suddanly thair come thocht greit power wo k striuiling brig tre sichand said na passage fault fude haue fastit lang weirmen think na tyme gang cambuskinneth sall watter till lat god aboue quhat land langer may nocht byde tary maid sumpart forthis syde tuik weid graithit mair swo band wounder scharply schair amang geir schulders loft thus went greit god prayand oft hie grace cause tak hand ouir watter swam south land arrayit sone sesoun richt cauld piscis dayis auld ouirthort kers torwod yeid ane wedow dwelt quhilk helpit neid hidder come day began daw ane windo priuatly caw thay speirit name bot tel yame wald nocht quhill scho hir self neir langage socht fra tyme scho wist wicht wallace reiosit scho thankit god grace scho speirit sone quhy allane murnand said man haue nane scho askit quhair men suld fair dame said ga get sum meit haue fastit sen yister day morne dreid full sair men forlorne greit part thame deith saw brocht scho gat meit haist scho mocht ane woman callit al hir ane chyld bad thame pa agane thay wayis wyld gask hall tythingis speir gif part war left men feir scho suld find ane hors sone hir gait bad thame se gif place stude stait thairof heir full greit desyre thocht fyre thay passit furth withouttin tary mair rest wallace remainit thair refreschit meit drink heit quhilk causit throw naturall cours sleip quhair suld sleip woman speirit wedow thre sonnis war leirit first twa thame scho send keip wallace gart thrid ga sone donypace tald eme hapnit thair persoun come se weilfair wallace sleip laid wod syde twa youg men without neir couth byde persoun come neir hand thair maner saw thay bekynnit quhat stede suld draw rone thick wallace sleipit yeid maid bot lytill dyn sa last ane sycht full priuatly quhair bed dicht beheld syne said vnto sell heir meruell quha lykis tell ane persoun worthines hand trowis stop power ingland fals fortoun miswirkar auenture he geuin ane fall left without supple ane cruell wyfe wapins micht la wallace hard yat sleip ouer past feirfly rais said al fast thow lei fals preist war thow ane fa wald dreid sic vther ten haue mair sen yisterday morne sic sextie war assemblit beforne eme tuke wet furth wallace tauld panefull cace nicht said left myne allane fell debait enemeis mony ane god he ay lyfe keip ouer forth swame awfull deip quhat haue weir befoir day presoun pane nicht bot play sa bet straikis sad sair schill watter brynt mekill mair efter greit blude throw heit cald wrocht lyfe almaist nathing rocht mene far mair tynsall men self micht suffer sic ten persoun said deir sone thow may se weill langer stryfe helpis nocht adeill thy men ar loist ane ryse goddis saik mak sall deuyse tak ane lordschip quhair thow may leif king edward greit landis geif vnkill said sic wordis na mair na thing bot iking cair lyke better se suthroun de gold land thay gif traist thow richt weill weir sall ceis vntill tyme bring scotland pei de thairfoir plane vnderstand sa come keirlie gude steuin ireland wedowis sone wallace yame brocht fra thay saw na sadnes thay rocht perfite ioy thay weipit thair ene ground thay fell thankit heuinis quene al glaid reskew thame twa thair feris leuand war left na thay tauld schir gerard deid thay weill eschapit steid throw oichell thay gane nicht erth ferry quhen day licht ane trew scot throw kyndnes wallace brocht thame one ouer syne kend thame plac al ke wist gif wallace leuand war neir ypais suld find thair persoun gart gude purueyace yame dicht torwod thay ludgit nicht quhill woman wallace north send returnit agane tauld ane end quhat inglismen way scho fand deid fell fallin fey mony sindrie steid hors scho saw wallace reft gask hall standand left withouttin harme steirit ane stane bot men gude tythingis scho gat nane thairfoir greuit greitly yde forest wald na langer abyde wedow gaif part siluer bricht twa hir sonnis worthie war wicht thrid scho left laikit age weir micht nocht wyn vassalage persoun gat thame gude hors geir bot wa mynd sa weir thus tuke leif without langer abaid dundaf mure samin nicht raid schir iohne ye grahame quhilk lord yat land ane agit knicht maid nane vther bad bot purchest peax rest micht byde still tribute payit full sair aganis sone baith wise worthie wicht alexander feirs berwik maid knicht quhair schawin battell haue bene betuix scottis bauld persee kene youg schir iohne richt nobill weir ane braid sword father gart sweir suld trew wallace thing quhill lyfe thame micht ring thre nychtis thair wallace dreid restit weill sa he mekle neid feird day wald na langer abyde schir iohne ye grahame bownit wt ryde said nay sulde ane plane part yit tak haue tynt men throw ouir reckles deid ane brynt chylde al mair sair fyre suld dreid freindis sumpart haue cliddisdaill ga se quhat thay may auaill schir iohne answerit counsall quhen ye think tyme send priuatly sall cum power haist betaucht vnto haly gaist sanct iohne borgh yai suld meit hail sound dundaf four couth found bothwell mure nicht remanit ane craufurd yat ludgit priuie vpon morne gilbank went ressauit mony glaid intent deir eme young anchinlek dwelt thair brother schiref air quhen auld schir ranald deid dicht anchinlek weddit lady bricht chylder gat storyis record lesmahago held lord bot slane pietie mair perseis men towne air sone dwelt still nyntene yeir age bruikit haill father heritage tribute payit landis braid lord persee brother maid leif wallace deir vnkill still inglismen yit sum thing speik ane messinger sone throw countrie yeid lord persee tauld felloun deid kincleuin brynt brokin cassin doun capitane deid sanct iohnstoun lorane al schortwod schawis schene land greit sorrow he bene sene throw wicht wallace yat deid he done towne spyit forthocht v sone butellar slane douchtie men deir asper sp iche persee speir quhat word pray graithly tell lord said richt thus cais befell knaw treuth left allane fled slew full mony ane hors fand yat yat gait couth beir bot self nane vther word heir striuiling brig wait passit nocht deith forth may v brocht lord perses said suithly war sin sa gude hand nane warld within tane peax bene kingis man haill impyre micht haue conquest yan greit harme knychtis ar deid mon gar se vther thair steid trow nocht yit wallace loissit clerkis sayis sall gar mony de messinger sayis full suith he bene mony hundreth cruell kene sen began ar loist without remeid persee said forsuith nocht deid cruikis forth knawis wounder weill lyfe sall natioun feill quhen stressit swome greit strenth he baith wit grace yairtill ane messinger lord chargit wend comand writ send schir iohne stewart gart schiref ya maid sanct iohnstoun landis braid kincleuin thair dwelt nane syne agane thair nocht bot brokin wallis plane leif thame thus reuland landis thair speik wallace glaid weilfair send keirlie vnto rannald nicht boyd blair worthie war wicht adame al cousing gude wallace thame declarit panefull cace eschaip company richt wounder glaid war thir gude cheualry fra tyme thay wist wallace leuand gude expensis thay maid pa maister iohne blair ane message ane worthy clerk baith wise richt sauage leirit befoir pareis toun amang maisteris science gude renoun wallace hame scule bene sone efterwart veritie sene man principall vndertuke first compylit dyte latine buke wallace lyfe richt famous renoun thomas gray persoun libertoun thay war put historiall oft ane baith mekill trauall thairfoir heir mak thame mentioun maister iohne blair wallace maid doun se heill comfort mo thay full oft togidder war befoir siluer gold thay gaif spend sa thame frely quhen god send gude weilfair wantit nane inglismen wist left allane quhair suld nane thame couth say drownit slane eschaipit away thairfoir thay tuke bot lytill heid thay knew nocht le dreid trew scottis greit fauour gaif quhat gude thay misterit nocht craif peax lestit schir rannald ta e thay thre monethis suld nocht gane haill cristmes wallace remanit thair lanerk oft sport maid repair quhen went gilbank fra toun gif fand men natioun scotland thay neuer greuance mair sum stikkit thay sum throttis sunder schair feill war fund deid bot nane wist quha quhome handlit leit na farther pa thair hessilrig dwelt yat cursit knycht waill schiref thay landis haill felloun outrage dispitefull deid mony thairfoir mekill dreid meruell thocht quha durst pepill la without toun gart greit number ga quhen wallace saw thay war nocht bot salust courtes ie al four men bure thame sa quyetlie na sutheroun culd deme yame vnhonestlie lanerk dwelt ane gentill woman thair ane madyn myld buik declair auchtene yeir auld lytill mair age al borne scho part heritage hir father worschip renoun hew braidfute hecht lamintoun feill countrie cald befoir tyme thay gentill men war ald bot gude man al wyfe deid madin wist nane vther remeid bot still scho dwelt tribute toun purchest king edward protectioun seruandis hir freindis hir thus leifit scho without desyre ill ane quyet hous scho micht hald weir hessilrig done hir mekill deir slane hir brother quhilk eldest air sufferit scho richt lawly hir bair amiabill sa bening war wyse courtes sweit fulfillit gentrice weill reullit toung richt haill countenance vertewis scho worthie auance humbill hir led purchest ane gude name alkin wicht scho keipit hir fra blame trew richteous folk ane greit fauour hir lent vpon ane day kirk scho went wallace hir saw eye cast prent lufe prunyeit last sa asperly throw beutie bricht greit vneis presence byde micht knew full weill hir kinrent hir blude scho honest vse gude quhyle wald think lufe hir ouir laif ane vther quhyle thocht desaif men war brocht confusioun throw last lufe sanct iohnstoun wald think leue lat ouir flyde bot thocht lang mynd micht nocht abyde tauld keirlie new lust baill syne askit trew counsall maister said al far haue feill liklynes may wounder weill sen ye sa lufe tak hir mariage gudely scho al he heritage suppois ye luifing feill ane mi greit god forbid suld sa mary thus nocht yit attend wald weir first se ane finall end na mair allane lufe gang tak tent dreid suffer wrang proffer lufe thus sone wald nocht preif micht leif weir think leif quhat lufe na thing bot fulischnes may reif baith wit steidfastnes said thus nocht graithly amouris weir atanis regne richt suith stude blis lufe quhair deidis war suld better prufe bot weill wait quhair greit ernist thocht lattis weir ye wysest man wrocht le gif bot erly till ane deid thinkis lufe speid may weill haue fortoun grace bot standis ane vther cace ane greit kinrik feill fais ouirset richt hard amendis get ani thame keip obseruance quhilk belangis lufe freuoll chance exempill haue forthinkis sair trow god sall sa na mair treuth knaw hir lynnage knew nocht hir thairfoir loissit ane gage keirlie thus arguit kynd bot greit desyre remaning mynd behauld frely fassoun ane quhyle left come nocht toun vther thing maid wit wa k preuand gif micht langour aik quhen keirlie saw sufferit pane thy deir schir said ye leif slogardy sa se lufe sall ye get com ort counsall walkit sport vnto kirk quhair scho maid residence scho knew weill bot eloquence scho durst nocht weill presence kyth full sair scho dred sutheroun suld hir myth hessilrig ane mater new begune hir desyrit mariage sone hir madin thus wallace scho besocht dyne hir priuatly scho brocht throw ane gardin scho gart wirk new sa inglismen nocht thair meting knew kissit may glaidly plesance sone hir besocht richt hartly acquentance scho answerit humbill wordis wyse war acquentance richt worthie pryse ye sall haue god saif saill bot inglismen garris power faill throw violence thame thair bairnage he weill neir distroyit lynage quhen wallace hard hir compleyne pieteously greuit hart richt gretumly baith ire lufe set ane rage bot nocht thy soberit curage mater tauld said air gudely lufe constraint sair scho answerit richt ressonablie agane said sall seruice bane plesance honest causis haill traist nocht ye wald set assaill worschip dishonour ane mayde standis mony stour fra inglismen saif womanheid coist he maid keip fra thair feid gude na lemman na man borne thairfoir think suld ye desyre nocht bot gudlynace perchance ye think war law percace attend richteous wyfe seruice wald vse lyfe heir beseik worschip armis ye charge nocht na vngodly harmis bot defend worschip blude quhen wallace weill hir trew taill vnderstude ane part thocht ressoun hir desyre thairfoir conclusioun thankit hir said gif micht throw goddis kinrik fre wald yow wed hartly plesance bot tyme may nocht tak sic chance cause nane vther craif ane man weir may nocht plesance haif thair talk tell yow na mair purpois quhat band thay maid thair conclude thay thus denner went sair greuance remanit intent lois n lustie pane lufe leif tuke tyme remufe phow wallace past lochmabane thay cuttit hors taillis schaif blude latter ca ij syne gilbank past nicht vpon ye morne four dicht corheid without resting raid quhair neuoy thom haliday abaid edward lytill al cou ing deir quhilk blyith quhen wist sa neir thankand greit god send thame saif agane mony demit stratherne slane gude cheir thay maid thay dayis thre wallace said desyrit se lochmabane toun inglismen yat yair feird day thay bownit thame fair sextene gudly cheualry knok wod leifit bot thre thomas haliday went town edward lytill keirly maid thame bown ane oistler thomas haliday led yame richt gaif command yair denner suld dicht heir ane me gude intent thay yeid inglismen thay trowit thair na dreid ane cliffurd come emis sone lord thre treuth record thair innis sone efter wallace past quha aucht thay hors greit hething ast gude wyfe said haue pleist best thre gentill men ar cumin west quha deuill thame maid sa gaylie ryde faith ane wed thair mon abyde thir lewit scottis he leirit lytill gude lo thair hors ar schent fault blude greit scorne outtin wordis mair taillis thay thre hors thay schair gude wyfe cryit pieteously couth greit sa wallace come couth capitane meit ane woman tauld thay hors schent proper ire grew matalent followit fast said gude freindis abyde seruice tak thy craft tyde marchell thow art without command reward agane think suld pay sen lait new come west countrie ane barbour best cut schaif ane wounder gude thow sall feill vse lat blude gude sword capitane he tane quhill hors agane merchellit neuer nane ane vther sone vpon heid straik quhill chaftis cheik vpon gait fle men tother thre slane thair hors thay tuke graithit yame ful bane town denner baid thay nane wyfe payit maid sa pieteous mane inglismen fra chiftane deid wallace socht fra mony sindrie steid castell come cruell men kene quhen wallace he thair suddand semblie sene towart sum strenth bownit ryde thocht na tyme b de hors bled fast gart dreding haif gude men wald haue laif knok wod withouttin mair thay ra bot na soiorning maid wod nouther thick strang men gat syne lichtit gang towart ane hicht led thair hors ane quhyle inglismen war within ane myle fresche hors rydand full haistely seuin scoir cumpany scottis lap quhen thay power saw frawart south thame thocht best draw wallace said na wit weir power byde thame bargane heir ne ar gude men thairfoir reid innermair seik quhill god send v supple haliday said sall counsaill bot sair dreid thir hurt hors aill inglismen burnist armour cleir thame approchit wounder neir horsit archearis schot wald nocht spair wallace men thay woundit twa full sair ire grew quhen saw thame bleid self turnit thame sone yeid sextene worthie weir formest richt scharply doun thay beir returne fyftene feild slane laif thay fled vnto thair power agane wallace followit gude cheualry thomas haliday weir full besy ane buschement saw cruell kene twa hundreth haill weill graithit inglismen vnkill said power smaw fra plane feild counsall yow draw ar aganis yone felloun staill wallace returnit full sone counsaill corheid full fane thay wald haue bene bot inglismen he weill thair purpois sene plane battell thame followit hardely danger thus thay held thame awfully hew morland wallace followit fast befoir maid mony scot agast haldin weir worthiest man north ingland thame leuand yam armour weill forgit fyne steill ane nobill cursour bure baith fast weill wallace returnit besyde ane burely aik set ane felloun sicker straik baith collar bane schulder blaid twa throw mid coist ye gude sword gart ga speir wan al cursour bricht syne left awin loissit micht laik blude micht na farther gang wallace hors sutheroun men amang men releuit douchtie war deid reskew felloun dreid cruell straikis forsuith thair micht sene ather syde quhill blude ran grene richt perrillous semblay see hardy hait continewit mellee schow reskew scottis inglis al sum keruit bane sunder sum hals sum hurt sum hynt sum doungin deid hardy scottis sa steirit steid haliday fute bauldly abaid amang sutherou ane ful greit rowme yai maid wallace hors hynt ane nobill speir throw thame raid gude chiftane weir thre slew thair speir gane thus gude sword hand he tane dang derf straikis sad sair quhome hit greuit scottis na mair fra sutheroun men naturall ressoun knew ane straik ay ane man slew meruellit thay sa mekill mane thair best man kynd slane greit strenth agane helpit nocht nane vther incontrair wallace socht said thay leif strenth vntane haill kinrik wyn allane thay left feild thair power fled tauld thair lord euill formest sped quhilk graystok hecht new cum ye land thairfoir trowit nane durst agane stand wounder thocht quhen yat saw sicht quhy gude men sa tuik flicht returne feild twentie war tynt morland al thairfoir wald nocht stynt bot followit fast thre hundreth dreid swore suld vengit deid scottis wan hors yair awin couth faill fleing syne cheisit maist auaill feild thus wicht wallace gane gude men loissit ane fyue woundit war lichtly furth thay raid wallace ane space behind yame ay abaid halyday preuit weill mony place sister sone gude wallace warly thay raid held thair hors aynd thay trowit weill sutheroun wald affaynd haill power atanis thame set bot wallace kest thair purpois let brek thair ray vesyit full fast inglismen sa greitly agast nane thame durst rusche staill array togidder held thame haill sutheroun saw abandounly wallace abaid neir hand thair cheualry morlandis hors yai knew wouder weill past thair lord tauld euer ilk deill lo schir thay said forsuith yone handis garris sa mony de haue hors grace vpon feit byde doutis nocht throw fyue thousand ryde reid ye ceis follow na mair dreid repent syne full sair blamit thame said men may weill se cowartis ye ar sa wald fle thair counsall yit leif wald thame nocht greit ire thame sadly socht waillad ane place quhair yai micht bargane mak wallace wa vpon tak sa byde thame ane plane quenisbery wald haue bene full fane vpon self tuke full greit trauell fend men gif micht auaill ane sword hand richt manlyke weir ay waittand fast gif micht get ane speir heir thair befoir thame fra hors gaif ouir micht na farther ga richt skirt quenisbery befell bot vpon grace myne author tell schir iohne ye grahame yat worthie wicht ye corheid come ye vther nicht threttie nobill men wage first douchter mariage haliday neuoy wallace tythingis speir schir iohne past ye place men speik quhair thay ane tryst set richt neir steid quhair scottis inglis met ane kirkpatrik cruell kene e daill wod half ane yeir bene inglismen tuld nocht weill accord torchorwald barroun lord kin wallace mother deir craufurd syde mekill steir twentie led worthie men wicht wallace approchit thair sicht schir iohne ye grahame quhe ye couter saw thame raid stude bot lytill aw gude father knew richt wounder weill kest doun speir sonyeit nocht adeill kirkpatrik al worthie men weir fyftie front atanis doun thay beir throw thickest thre hundreth thay raid sutheroun syde ull greit slauchter yai maid thame reskew felloun thrang wallace fute greit power amang gude rowme gat throw help goddis grace sutheroun fled left thame place horsis thay wan stuf chace gude speid wallace douchtie war deid graystok tuke flicht sterne hors stout ane hundreth held togidder ane rout wallace thame full sadly culd persew fleing weill inglismen knew ay best wald pa thair chiftane befoir ad gude schir iohne ye grahame ay strykand doun quhome euer micht hy wallace said bot waist foly commounis slay quhair chiftanis gais away ho ar fresche thairfoir say gude men ye haue ar yit nobill stait yone greit rout godis lufe hald gait sinder thame sone sall cum hand quhen schir iohne taill weill vnderstad nane vther fra thynefurth tuke heid formest followit weill gude speid kirkpatrik al considderit thair counsaill thay chargit thair men ay follow staill command full sone thame thay met sad straikis air sadly vpon thame set schir iohne grahame graystok fast socht pesane yan helpit richt nocht vpon craig ane graith straik gat richt burly blaid braid burnist bricht sunder ker mailyeis fyne steill throw braun bane ruschit euerilk deill deid dynt groud doun draif wallace assemblit laif derflie deith feill freikis thair dicht rais neuer agane quha euer hit richt kirkpatrik thom haliday thair men thair douchtie deidis war nobill ken knok heid bald graystok slane mony men quhilk war mekill mane saif thair lyfis part wod thay past scottis men thay ran togidder fast quhe wallace schir iohne ye grahame met richt gudly hubilnes gret perdoun askit reprufe oir chace said suld moir informatioun mak sa gude quhen schir iohne wallace weill vnderstude way said yairof na mair ye full richt weill fair wyser weir ye ar father armis ye ar thy kirkpatrik syne cousing deir thankit richt ane gude maneir nocht ane loist thair cheualry schir iohne ye grahame yame come happily day done approchand nicht wallace thay askit counsall richt answerit thus speik bot leif richt laith war ony gude man greif bot thus say termis schort wald assaill gif ye think may lochmabane hous quhilk left allane weill wait power nane carlauerok al yit maxwell he hand thay micht baith ane wand aganis sutheroun he countrie say quhat ye best think schir iohne grahame gaif first gude co sent syne ye laif richt ane hail intent lochmabane richt haistely thay ryde quhen yai come yair nocht half ane myle besyde nicht mirk counsall ar thay gane mone sterne apperance yair nane wallace said think land rest thom haliday thow knawis countrie best heir na noyis feill folk heir thairfoir trow ar le dout haliday said tak ane ryde befoir maner se watsone callit thow mak bown yame thow ay nichtbour yi town grant thame aganis myne intent euer thame ill vnto yet thay twa peirtly furth raid portar come without langer abaid iohne watsone tythingis culd speir oppin bad capitane cumis neir ye mair vnwysely vp drew thom haliday sone craig threw ane knyfe stikkit deid ane dark hoill doun dreidles kest deid iohne watsone he hynt keyis hand portar ya wicht wallace cumand thay enterit befoir thame fand na except wemen simpill seruandis twa kiching lang scudlaris thay bene sone thay war slane quhen lady sene scho cryit grace deit tre wallace said madame noyis lat wemen yit bot lytill euill young childer lyke nocht spill wald haue meit haliday quhat sayis thow fastand folk dyne gude tyme war greit pur iance ordanit thame befoir baith breid aill gude wyne vther stoir meit thay bownit thay fastit lang gude men armis vnto clois gart gang part fleand folk fute thay fra thame glaid knok heid quhair greit melle maid ay thay come iohne watsone leit thame done deith without noyis din na man left thair ingland borne castell weill thay vesyit morne iohnstoun send ane man gude degre secund dochter forsuith weddit halidayis deir neuoy wallace greit capitane thay maid place thay left thair ane gude array syne ischit furth vpon secund day wemen leif ingland fair schir iohne ye grahame gude wallace culd cair corheid ludgit yame yat nicht vpon morne sone hicht efter denner thay wald na langer byde thair purpois tuke craufurd mure ryde schir iohne ye grahame wallace yat wicht thom haliday agane returnit richt corhall thair remanit dreid na sutheroun wist principall quha yi deid kirkpatrik past eskdaill woddis wyde saiftie thair thocht suld abyde schir iohne ye grahame gude wallace feir thame fourtie men armis cleir throw craufurd mure thay tuke ye way inglismen thair mynd remanit ay phow wallace wan ye castel craufurd slew capitane thairof ca iij fra craufurd iohne ye watter doun yai ryde neir hand nicht thay lichtit vpon clyde thair purpois tuke ane quyet vaill wallace said wald micht assaill craufurd castell sum gude ieopardie schir iohne ye grahame say ye best may gude knicht said ye men war without tak hous thair bot lytill dout ane squyar reullit lordschip haill cubirland borne name mortindaill wallace said self pa feir ane herbery speir follow dreich gif myster ocht edward lytill maister furth soche ane ostillary ane woman met scho tauld yame yat sutheroun yair set ye scottis counsall yow pa thay may ye get euill herbery drink thay ar sa haue thay bene richt lang greit word thair wallace thame amang thay trow he fund men agane lochmabane feill inglismen slane hous tynt garris thame full wa trow god thay sall sone tyne wallace speirit scotland gif scho scho said yee thinkis se sorrow thame throw help goddis grace askit hir quha place na man fence left hous within twentie ar heir mak greit noyis din allace scho said gif micht ani se worthie scottis maist maister woman wald na langer stand ane bekin maid schir iohne come wallace went said benedicite capitane speirit quhat bella ny may thow cumis sa grym sum tything v tel thow art ane scot deuill thy natioun quel wallace braid sword withouttin mair breist brym capitane bair throw coist stikkit id ane vther hit akwart vpon heid quhome euer straik bris bane lyre feill thame deit fell flatlingis fyre haistie payment maid thame lure edward lytill keipit weill dure schir iohne ye grahame fane wald haue bene edward bad castell begin thir folk haue bot lytill dreid schir iohne ye grahame fast castell yeid wallace rudely sit routis thame gaif thay twentie men derfly deith thay draif fyftene straik fyftene he slane edward slew fyue quhilk mekill mane castell wallace greit desyre schir iohne set hous fyre nane thair greit defence culd bot wemen fast sair weip wa without place ane auld bulwark maid wallace yeid ouir withouttin langer abaid wemen sone saifit fra deid waik folk put barnis fra steid purueyance fand lytill nane befoir yat tyme thair victuall gane yit place thay ludgit nicht fra oistillary brocht sic gude thay micht vpon morne housis thay spulyeit fast thing docht place thay cast treme wark yai brynt yat war within yai vanis wallis brak doun stalwart war stanis spilt thay micht syne wald na langer byde vnto dundaf samin nicht thay ryde ludgit thair mirth plesance thankand greit god yat lent yame sic gude chace p pin sext buik declarit spousage wallace hessilrig slew wallace wyfe toun lanerk ew hessilrig samin cause put inglismen lanerk passit octauis februar part marche richt degestioun appeirit last moneth ver signe somer sweit sesoun wallace fra dundaf maid boun leif tuke kilbank fair rumour rais throw scotland vp doun inglismen wallace leuand wair apryle quhen cleithit wene abill ground throw wirking natour wodd he yair worthie weid grene quhen nympheus beilding bour oyle balme fulfillit sweit odour canetti race thay war wont gang walkand thair cours euerie casuall hour glaid huntaris thair mery sang tyme approchit new lustie pane quhilk spak air luifis cace thocht persew lanerk toun hidder fair residence ane quhyle remanit thair hir presence haue said befoir thocht inglismen greuit repair yit desyrit thing set soir fyre lufe reullit sic wyse lykit weill gudely quhylis wald think danger ryse vther quhylis hir presence fle ceis weir war best thus win nocht bot sadnes ilk syde sall neuer man cowardnes se weir chance may betyde quhat lufe bot greit mischance wald bring fra armis verrily nocht change worschip plesance weir think tyme occupy yit hir lufe nocht let thy mair sall desyre worschip refer fra day furth euer mair feir weir quhidder leif sterf quhat suld say wallace planely set lufe hir best warid sa wyde thinkand suld desyre get sa befell concord ane tyde scho maid command byde thus began stynting stryfe band begun graith witnes besyde myne author sayis scho weddit wyfe leif peax leif gude concord leif play leif haill plesance scho chance he baith hir lufe lord thankis lufe sa auance sa eninly held fauour ballance sen may lap hir armis scho thankit god hir hie happy chance tyme flour armis fortoun schew hir figurit doubill face feill syse bene set abufe presoun deliuerit throw grace vneis vnrest rufe weill weild plesand lufe thocht self aduersitie desyrand ay manheid prufe curage set vpon stagis hie verray treuth nocht graithly tell lyfe lang thay bene throw naturall cours generatioun fell ane chylde cheuit thir twa luifaris betwene quhik gudelie ane madin bricht schene sa farther furth become tyme hir age ane squyar schaw yat yan full weill he sene lyfe lait man gat hir mariage vther maid weddit ane squyar wicht quhilk weill knawin cummin balliollis blude thair airis lyne succedit richt lamintoun vther landis gude mater richt quha vnderstude heirof na mair proceid sentence schortly conclude vther thing purpois reid richt gudely men come lady ying farther thame speik na mair bot wallace furth weir ring micht nocht ceis greit curage sa bair sutheroun slay dreid wald nocht spair thay oft syse feill causis wrocht fra tyme furth quhilk mouit mair sair neuer warld mynd brocht leif thy myrth leif thy haill plesance leif thy blis leif thy chyldis age leif thy youth follow thy hard chance leif thy lust leif thy mariage leif thy lufe thow sall tyne ane gage quhilk neuer eird salbe redemit agane felloun fortoun hir feirs outrage go leif weir go leif cruell pane fy fortoun fy thy freuoll quheill fy thy traist heir he lest sa trasfigurit wallace weill quhen traistit haue leuit best plesance heir bot ane gest throw thy feirs cours he na hap ho thow ouirthrew lykand rest fra greit plesance weir trauell wo quhat fortoun quha drawis dait sa fast wait thair baith weill wickit chance bot fals warld mony doubill cast nocht bot verray variance na thing heuinly gouernance pray maker abufe quhilk he iustice ballance v grant deir lestand lufe pheirof farther speik na mair bot purpois schortly fair tvelf hundreth yeir thairto nyntie seuin fra christ borne richteous king heuin williame wallace gude lyking gais lanerk toun amang mortall fais inglismen euer fals he bene hessilrig quhilk cruell kene robert thorne ane felloun subtile knicht he fund way quhat mene best thay micht thay suld mak contrary wallace argument come vpon cace fra kirk without toun quhill thair power micht armis boun schir iohne ye grahame yat worthie trew lanerk toun gude wallace persew weilfair full oft sene gude men cumpany fyftene wallace nyne thay war na feiris vpon morne vnto me ga thay thair men graithit gudely grene sosoun sic vse full lang he bene quhen sadly thay said thair deuotioun ane arguit thame thay went throw toun starkest man hessilrig knew al lichtly wordis anew salust thame war bot scorne dew gard gude day bone senyeour gude morne quhome scornis thow quod wallace quha leirit thee quhy schir said come ye ouir ye see pardoun weind ye bene ane ambaxat bring ane vncouth quene wallace answerit sic pardoun haif v gif thy part thow sall nocht craif sen ye ar scottis yit salust sall ye gud euin daucht lord ballanch banyeochade sutheroun men thame assemblit neir wallace laith mak ane steir ane maid ane skrip tit lang sword hald still thy hand quod sp ik thy word thy lang sword thow makis mekill boist thairof quod thy dame maid lytill coist quhat cause he thow weir yat gudely grene maist cause bot mak tene quhat suld ane scot sa fair ane knyfe said preist last ianglit thy wyfe woman lang he callit sa fair quhill chylde worthit thyne air think quod thow dryfis scorne thay dame iapit thow borne power assemblit twa hundreth men stalwart war stout scottis saw thair power cumand schir robert thorne hessilrig hand greit multitude wappinis burneist bene worthie scottis quhilk cruell war kene amang sutheroun sic dyntis gaif tyde quhill blude breid bristit fra woundis wyde wallace stour cruelly fechtand ane sutheroun smoit richt hand quhen carll fechting micht na air left hand ire held ane buklair fra stump blude sprang ful fast wallace face aboundantly cast greit part marrit sicht schir iohne ye grahame ane straik he tane richt gude sword vpo ye sutheroun syre derfly deith draif ire perrell richt awfull hard strang stour indurit meruellously lang inglismen yit gadderit wounder fast worthie scottis gait left last quhen thay flane woundit mony ane wallace innis ganest way thay gane thay passit sone defendit thame richt weill schir iohne swordis stif steill behind thair men quhill thay yet tane woman quhilk full wane perrell saw felloun noyis din set vp yet leit thame enter throuch ane strenth thay passit steid fyftie sutheroun vpon gait lay deid fair woman besynes micht inglismen tary ane slicht quhill wallace wod past cartlane craigis thay persewit full fast quhe sutheroun saw yat chaipit wallace agane thay turnit woman tuke cace put hir deith nocht tell yow sic mater may nocht tarie quhair greit dule redeming agane renewing bot eiking pane ane trew woman seruir hir full lang toun ganest way gang wallace tauld deid done panefull wo socht hart full sone war nocht schame schot ground bitter baill breist bound schir iohne ye grahame baith wyse gentil fre greit murning maid pietie se al laif war assemblit thair pure sorrow hart weipit full sair quhen wallace feld thair curage sa small fenyeit comfort thame ceis men said ane buteles pane nocht cheueis hir lyfe agane vneis ane word micht bring tene bailfull teiris brist braithly fra ene sichand said sall neuer man se rest eis quhill deid wrokin sarkles slauchter hir baith blyith bricht awow maker micht natioun sall neuer forbeir young auld abill weir preist woman think nocht sla default bot gif thay causing schir iohne said lat murning hir saik thair sall ten thousand de quhair men may weip thair curage le slaikis ire wrang thay suld redres tyme ly hous full fane wald haue bene nicht mirk yit wallace he sene feirfly straik come greit ice vpon heid bristit throw bane lira scheirand sword glaid schulder bane ouir stair amang thame gane gude chinlek trowit nocht deid thryis ane knyfe straik steid scry rais rudely streit feill laif war ful yeit vnder feit young hessilrig wicht wallace met ane sicker straik williame he set derfly deith ouir stair dang doun mony nicht thay slew lanerk toun sum greissis lap sum stikkit within affeirit thay war hiddeous noyis din schir iohne ye grahame set ye hous fyre quhair robert thorne brynt vp bane lyre twelf scoir thay slew yat war ingland borne wemen thay leuit preistis morne pa thair way blis gudis bair swore thay agane suld cum na mair quhen scottis hard thir fyne tythingis new partis wallace fast thay drew pleneist toun quhilk thair heritage thus wallace straif aganis greit barnage ay began stryfe stalwart hand cheueis agane sum rowmis scotland worthie scottis semblit thair cheis cheif thair chiftane leidair aymer wallange ane felloun tyran knicht wel dwelt king edward ful richt murray thocht richteous lord land trew men record arrane dwelland tyde vther land durst nocht byde bot fals knicht well w mand ane man gart sone king edward pa tauld haill wallace ordinance put pepill mischance planely rissin agane ring greuit thair richt greitly king throw ingland gart doaris cry power get said wald planely scotland pa realme statute new feill men weir richt fast thay drew quene feld weill purpois scho went kneis syne scho wald desist nocht scotland gang ye suld haue dreid wirk sa felloun wrang cristinit thay ar yone thair heritage reif thair croun ane greit outrage hir counsall hame wald nocht byde lordis feit scotland ryde ane scottis yan dwelt king edward quhen hard fell wallace tuke sic part stall fra thame al priuatly may scotland come vpon ane day seikand wallace maid reddy boun scot borne kyle ricardtoun ingland coist knew wounder weill fra hull bristow euerie deill fra carlile throuch sandwiche yat royall steid fra douer ouir vnto sanct bayis heid picardy flanders baith bene normandy france he sene purseuant king edward weir bot culd neuer gar armis beir greit stature sumpart gray inglismen callit bot grymisbie wallace come kyle fand tauld haill tythingis ingland thay turnit name fra tyme yat knew callit iop ingyne trew tyme gude seruice fand gaif beir armis scotland wallace agane cliddisdaill sone raid power semblit withouttin baid gart command quha wald pear tak ane fre remit suld gar mak alkin deid thay done beforne perseis peice schir rannalds worne feill drew bauldly durst abyde wallace kyn mony diuers syde schir rannald send power haill self durst nocht knawin battall agane sutheroun maid ane band lang tyme befoir hald thame land adame wallace past ricardtoun robert boyd gude men renoun cuninghame kyle come men waill lanerk socht hors ane thousand haill schir iohne ye grahame gude cheualrie schir iohne tynto yat micht gude auchinlek wallace vnkill mony trew scot yair chiftane culd pa thre thousand haill lyklie men weir feill fute quhilk wantit hors g ir tyme cumand vpon hand awfull oist edward ingland pthe battell bigar bigar come sextie thousand men weir weidis cruell ken thay plantit thair feill tentis pauillonis quhair clarion blew mony michtie sound pleneist place gude victuall wyne cartis brocht thair purueyance full fyne awfull king gart twa heraldis brocht gaif thame command haist thay mocht charge wallace suld cum till without promis put becaus wait ane gentill man cum grace sall saif lyfe vpon tak efter gif wald seruice mak sall haue wage may weill suffice rebald wenis he done supprise pepill oft vpon auenture aganis may lang indure proffer ganestandand gif heir awow salbe vangit hie ane young squyar brother schir hew thocht wald ga disagysit persew wallace se tuke sa hie ane part borne sister sone king edward ane coit armis tuke baid heraldis full priuatly furth raid tynto hill withouttin residence quhair wallace lay folk defen ane likly oist sa thay fand thay socht wald na langer stand gif ye reullis thing credence haue brocht fra worthie king wallace gart thre knichtis call syne red writ presence thame thame said answer ye sall nocht craif word writ quhilk lyks yow best haif wryt thay said war liklyest wallace thus began dyte haist pthow euar king yow chargis throw cace suld cum put thy grace gif ganest thow hechtis hing awow god euer may tak thow salbe hangit ane exempill geif king reif al lang may leif thow profferis thy wagis haif defy power laif helpis heir thy fals natioun god thow salbe put regioun de thairfoir contrair thocht thow sworne thow sall v se nyne houri morne battell gif maugre thy kyn falsly thow seikis realme within wri gaif heraldis mair gude reward gart delyuer thame thair bot iop knew weil ye squyar youg schir hew tauld wallace euer trew thame commandit thay suld sone tak self began sair accusing mak squyar said sen thow he fenyeit armis sall fall sumpart thir harmis exempill gif thy fals natioun vpon ane hill gart syne set doun straik heid wald farther go herald said syne withouttin ho thow art fals armis manesworne throw thy cheikis thy toung salbe schorne quhen done thrid said armis iudge thow sall neuer graithly se gart ane smyth turcas richt thair pull ene syne gaif thame leif fair fals king thy fellow sall leid thy answer turs neuoyis heid thus sair dreid king boist dum fellow led vnto thair oist quhe king edward heraldis thus he sen proper ire woxe neir wod tene wist nocht quhat wyse wreik sorrow maist ane word culd nocht speik ane lang quhyle stude wrythand ane rage loud said ane fell outrage deid scottis full deir salbe bocht sa dispitefull warld neuer wrocht fra regioun think nocht gang quhill tyme sall se rebell hang lat thus syte sorrow dwell gude scottis schortly tell fvrth fra men wallace raikit richt callit schir iohne tynto ye knicht leit wit vesy wald ga inglis oist bad tell na quhat euer thay speirit quhill yat come agan wallace disagy thus ownit ouir ane pla e betuix culter bigar past sone war quhair ane warkman come fast dryuand ane meir pitcheris sell gude freind said treuth thow tell schillingis wallace said thow sall haif haue meir pitcheris laif thy gowne hois haist thow put syne mak ane change sall gif myne thy auld hude threid air man wend weill scornit thair thow tary nocht sauld best fourtie pennyis said quhill thay may lest sum brak ane part sum prikkit ee wallace slaid priuatly leit thame vnto oist agane passit richt men tane tynto knicht schir iohne ye grahame gart leuch said forgif yow ar ye weirmen repentis sa small thay rewit v nocht toun air trew barrounis quhen yat yai hangit yair abirdene saifly thay pa quhair inglismen besy flittand ane hundreth schippis yat ruther buir air turs thair gudis hauin byd thair bot wallace oist come thame suddandly thair schaipit nane greit nauy bot feill seruandis thame leuit nane ane eb sey scottis thame gane tuik geir syne set schippis fyre men land thay brynt baith bane lyre yeid nane away bot preistis wyfis barnis maid thay debait thay chaipit nocht harmis buchane wallace maid ryde quhair lord bewinout ordanit abyde erll maid bot schort tyme befoir bruikit nocht busteous schoir quhen wist weill wallace cumand left land couth slanis pa syne schip fled ingland agane wallace raid throw north land plane cromarrie feill inglismen thay slew worthy scottis vnto couth persew returnit agane come abirdene biyith oist vpon lammes euin stabillit land thocht best suld syne ane oist passit dundie phow wallace laid ane seige dundie gait battel brig end striuiling kirkinghame yat thesaurar edward king ye erll warrane ca iiij gart set ane seige castell strang leif thair farther gang schir aymeir wallage haistir full fast ingland haill houshald past bothwell left murray heritage tuik bot king edwardis wage thus awin land forsuik euer mair wallace deid greit tythingis tald thair al inglismen sair murnit thair mude loissit heir baith lyfe landis gude edward couth nocht scotland fair bot kirkinghame thesaurair ane lord erll warrane chargit thame numberis mony ane richt weill besene scotland ryde tyme bypast incressit moir bot throw ane cace hapnit wyfe dunbar fra scho held stryfe throw supple wallace plane bot meane gat castell agane lang tyme yit couth nocht ceis agane wallace preuit mony preis inglismen suppleit thame micht contrair scotland yai wrocht full greit vnricht thair musture awfull se fechtand men thousandis war sextie striuiling brig past thay lykit byde erll malcolme ane seige thay laid yat tyde thocht keip command thair king bot gude wallace wrocht ane vther thing dundie left maid ane gude chiftane twa thousand keip hous stane north land men dwellaris dundie samin nicht sanct iohnstoun went vpon morne schiref mure raid thair ane quhyle gude array baid schir iohne ye grahame said haif vndertane le power sic thing weill gane tha wallace said quhair sic thing nixt fecht withouttin let setterday vnto brig thay raid gude plane buird weill ioyntly maid gart wachis wait nane suld thame pa ane wricht tuik subtillest thair ordanit saw buird twa myd trest nane micht ouir ga charnall bandis naillit full sone syne fillit clay na thing bene done tother end ordanit suld stand vpon rollaris tre quhen ane war laif doun suld fall self vnder ordanit thair bund trest ane cradill sit lous pyn quhen wallace leit wit bot ane horne quhen tyme oist na man suld blaw bot day approchit greit battall inglismen power wald nocht faill ay sex thay war agane ane wallace fyftie thousand maid thame battell place remanent baid castell still baith feild hous thay thocht tak worthy scottis vpon tother syde plane feild tuik fuit maid thame byde hew kirkinghame vangard led twentie thousand lyklie men se threttie thousand erll warrane bot wyse man bad first oist befoir ouir send sum scottis man weill maner kend bad wallace blaw said thay war anew haistit nocht bot sadly couth persew quhill warranis oist thick brig saw fra iop horne hint couth blaw sa asperly warnit gude iohne wricht rollar straik greit slicht laif yeid doun quhen pynnis gais ane hiddeous cry amang gaif ouir micht na farther gang wallace grahame euer togidder baid hadingtoun full greit slauchter thay maid inglismen quhen thair hors tyrit quhen rasay come gude wallace ful glaid boyd richard lundy yeildis sall neuer ransonit barrounis answerit worthely said thay wald pa thair cheualry self iop prouydit menye twentie thousand waillit men tuik harnes hors gart amang thame waill wappinnis anew regioun may comfort call manly hector wrocht weir aganis ane hundreth comptit speir bot nocht throw strenth anerly sic reull led nobill cheualry thir exemplis war worthy ken hector leif speik furth meruellit gif suld wallace without assouerance come persew place schir rauf gray sone presence couth warnit thus farther wald pa purpois ingland ryde na tyme haif seissing byde tak tent heir cuming agane gif ouir hous send keyis plane thus command befoir thir witnes large gif thow nocht remane charge bot done throw force tak ouir wall thow sall hangit hie turnit oist wend ilk command berwik sone send gude ramsay yat ane worthy knicht oist mair full awfully dicht began tweid spairit nocht thay fand bot brynt force haill northumberland durame toun thay brynt vp ane gleid abbayis thay spairit kirkis quhair yat yai yeid york thay raid baid thay wald blyn byrne slay thame thocht na syn na sin thay thocht samin lat v feill bot williame wallace quit querrell weill forthis thay wan small castellis kest doun asper wappinnis payit thair ransoun presoneris thay lykit nocht keip quhome yai ouir tuik thay maid thair freindis weip na sutherousauit yair greit rich sic trustrie callit bot wretchitnes vnto yettis subuerbis toun braithly yai brynt brak yair biggingis doun wallis assailyeit fyftene dayis quhil king edward scud yame wayis ane knicht ane clerk ane squyar pei prayit fair byrning ceis hecht battell fyftene dayis war past souerance sa lang gif lykit ast al speirit quhy wallace tuik hand felloun stryfe defence scotland said meruellit wit thy aganis ingland sa greit party sen ye haue maid mekill scotland fre war gude tyme lat malice wallace he hard message say thair manly voce richt thus said thame il ye may knaw weill richt aneuch haif souerance keip nocht craif becaus ane natiue scottis man det fend kingrik dangering desyre grant sum thing oist sall ceis chance may betyde thir fyftene dayis bargane abyde sall nocht le mufe yow respite self couth neuer trow king edwardis writ vnder seill yai gaif fourtie dayis thay suld battelll hait wallace gaif credence thair king thair leif thay tuik syne passit resting tald haill wallace leit thame feill yair souerance keipit nocht adeill sic reullit men sa awfull effeir ar nocht cristinit leidis weir king answerit said suld kend cumis wit enemeis commend thay ar dreid richt greitly certane sadly thay think harmis thay haue tane leif thame thus counsall thair king scottis agane speik sum thing vallace tranoyntit vpon secund day fra york yai past richt ane gude array north west yai went battell buskit boun thair ludgeing tuik besyde northallartoun cryit peax thair mercatis stand thay fourtie dayis pepill ingland quha lykit ony vittall sell thair schoir war mekill tell schir rauf rymont capitane miltoun greit power nicht ordanit pa wallace oist mak sum ieopardie feill scottis men dwelt countrie wist thing gadderit wallace thay maid wyse felloun cace gude lundy callit thair hew ye hay lochorquhart air thre thousand yat worthely wrocht syne priuatly fra oist thay socht men tuik come new gydis thay cuntrie knew oist maid gude quyet ane space fra thame buskit priuatlie schir rauf rymot seuin thousand come wallace oist ane ieopardie begin buschment brak thay oist come neir sutheroun men ye worthy scottis ca eir thre thousand hail war braithly brocht groud iourney thay socht sickerly he found schir rauf rymont stikkit ane speir thre thousand slane worthy war weir sutheroun wist quhen thair chiftane slane miltoun fast yai fled thair mane wallace followit gude cheualry amang sutheroun thay enterit suddanly scottis inglis toun atanis sutheroun men schot braithly kest doun stanis thair awin men richt feill thair haue yai slane scottis war mekill mane vp greissis ran seisit toun derfly deith sutheroun dang thay doun wallace thair he fundin full greit rich iowellis gold wappinnis harnes spulyeit toun wyne vittaill oist send cariage greit waill thre dayis still within toun baid syne brak doun werk worthely maid wyfis barnis thay put toun na man sauit natioun quhen scottis tane tursit thair desyre wallis thay brak set laif fyre tymmer werk thay brynt vp plane feird day oist raid agane gart cast ane dyke micht sum strenthing keip oist fra suddand ieopardie inglismen richt greitly agast fra north south vnto thair king yai past punfrayt lay held ane parliament gif battell lordis couth nocht consent bot wallace war scotland crownit king thair counsall fand ane perrillous thing thocht thay wan thay wan bot thay wair gif thay tynt loist ingland euer mair cace war put scottis hand decreit thair wit amang thame fand gif wallace wald vpon tak crown gif battaill thay suld reddy boun samin message thay send agane thair intent thay tald plane wallace thame chargit fra presence absent counsall callit schew thame intent men desyrit battell haif ony wyse ingland ouir laif self said first war ane ouir hie thing aganis faith reif richteous king man borne natiue scotland weir crown nocht tak hand send realme det skill lat god abone reward sum bad wallace vpon tak crown wyse men said nay war derisicun crown king voce parliament thay wist nocht gif scotland wald consent vther sone said wrangous place thus demit thay mony diuers cace knicht campbell wit ane worthy man said air thame present hard answerit quhen mony said thair war best wald wallace grant thair till crown king solempnitly ane day get ane end lang delay gude erll malcolme said yat wallace micht ane day fence scotlandis richt thocht refuissit lestandly beir ressaue crown feir weir pepill gaif thair consent malcolme ald lord parliament yit wallace thoillit leit thame say yair quhen thay demit mony diuers skill awin mynd abhorrit thing comounis cryit mak wallace crownit king semblit said suld nocht termis schort ye get na mair vnder cullour answer man mak bot sic ane thing nocht tak yow suffer say swa war ane scorne crown ta thay wald nocht lat message ingland cum thame amang thay suld vnderstand twa knichtis past message agane maid yame trow wallace crownt plane gart yame traist weil yat yi suithfast thing deliuerit thus thay passit king punfret went tald thay sene wallace crownit quhairof yai lordis war tene barrat wox parliament quhair thay stude said thay thir tythingis ar nocht gude sa weill thir tymes befoir thair king mekill moir ane fortunate man na thing gais agane gif battell sall repent pane ane vther said battell haue stroy land na tresour may v saue conquest sen first couth begyn sellis nocht bot takis may wyn inglismen settis na dome bot deid price pennyis may mak v na remeid ane wodstok sayis ye wirk nocht wyse gif ye tak anter suppryse thocht wyn ar ingland laif ar stark aganis v stand wallace saif vther thay compt bot small thy think war best keip strenthis castellis wallit toun sa sall fend folk regioun thocht north brynt better souerance set ingland ane ieopardie thay grantit wodstok thame say thus thay put battell delay kest thame haill vther gouernance aganis wallace wirk sum ordinance thus wallace he plane discomfeist haill aganis king edward haill battall throw falset subtilitie thay thocht suld greit necessitie decreit thay gaif parliament scottis furth speik myne intent wallace lay still quhill fourtie dayis war gane abydand thame bot apperance saw nane battell haue thair promeis maid gart display agane baner braid repreuit edward richt greitly thing bauchillit seill blew fals king recryand turnit bak yeid gait wallace maid full mony biggingis hait thay raissit fyre brynt vp northallartoun agane throw york schyre baldly maid yame bost distroyit land al far euer thay ryde seuin myle thay brynt ather syde wrocht ye sutherou mony werkad wound palicis spilt greit towris confound wedowis weipit sorrow thair sang madynnis murnit greit mening amang thay spairit nocht bot wemen kirk worthy scottis laubour wald nocht irk gaif abbayis richt largely thair gude kirk men thay na thing bot gude temporall land thay spuilyeit thair gude gardingis gay greit orchartis yai spil york thay went thir weirmen renoun ane seige thay set richt sadly toun greit defence thay garneist thame within ane felloun salt without thay begin pthe seige york ca iiij deuydit oist four partis wachis fell na man suld isch abone toun vpon south part syde thair wallace wald gude lundy abyde erll malcolme syne west yet abaid ye boyd yat gude iourneyis maid knicht campbell lochow yat lord north yet ramsay maid thame ford schir iohn ye grahame yat worthy weir auchinlek craufurd full manly effeir eist port baldly thay boun byde ane thousand archearis vpon scottis syde le erit thame amang four party fyue thousand bowman toun thy within wallis arrayit thame full richt twelf thousand semelie sicht said wallace yone war ane plane feild fecht think suld fane sailyeit thay richt fast euerie syde worthy scottis baldly durst abyde speir scheild gunnis bad ya nane within dykis yai gart feill sutheroun grane arrowis thay schot richt feirs ony fyre ouir wallis flawmit greit ire throw birneis bricht heidis fyne steill sutheroun blude freindschip nane yai feil schynand harnes schot blude sa schene inglismen cruell war kene keipit thair toun fendit thame full fast faggaldis fyre amang oist thay cast pik tar feill sowis thay lent mony war hurt thay fra wallis went stanis springhaldis thay cast sa fast gaddi irne maid mony grome agast bot neuertheles scottis yat war without toun full oft thay set greit dout thair bulwerk brynt richt brymly toun thair barmkin wan greit garrettis kest doun thus sailyeit thay ilk syde greit micht day gane cumin nicht wery oist drew thame fra toun set wachis resting maid thame boun wisch woundis wyne yame yat vnsoud nane deid greit mirth yai aboud feill men war hurt bot na murning thay maid confermit seige steidfastly thay baid quhen sone morrow rais vp bricht befoir chiftanis assemblit thay full richt said amendis toun thay suld tak fence yat suther un micht mak arrayit agane thay began befoir toun thay sailye wounder soir felloun schot ouir wallis full schene feill inglismen cruell war kene schot war slane thair targis strang bristit helmys mony ground thay dang brym byrnand fyre thay kest euerie yet entres thus perrell oft thay set defendaris war full greit defence keipit thair toun throw strenth violence thus day thay draif vnto nicht pauillounis bownit mony wery wicht irk weir toun strang win artailye nobill men within quhen yai trowit ye scottis war rest ieopardy inglismen thame kest schir iohne mortoun knawin worthy wicht schir william lei graithit yame ye nicht fyue thousand weill garnist sauage vpon scottis thay thocht mak skirmage yet ischit haistely erll malcolme gude cheualry chak wache wallace ten he bene rydand he thair cuming sene gart ane blaw cumpany reddy men arrayit thame haistely feill scottis ilk nicht harnes baid ordinance thay sic reull maid schort auyse togidder ar thay went vpon yair fais quhair feil sutherou war schent wallace knew weill erll haistie thy sped preis pa ane sword weir hand bair first hit craig sunder schair ane vther akwart face tuik baith neis front feild gart fle hardy erll befoir men past preis quhair feill war fechtand fast ane scheirand sword bair drawin hand first tey befoir fand quhen wallace togidder set thair lest nane agane thame thay met bot outher deid elli dynt fyne steill auaillit nocht wallace hand sen arthur na maik quhome richt hit ay deid ane weill knawin mony place quhome wallace hit yai detrit ye scottis na al men cruelly weill come straik yat micht ye sutherou inglismen fled leit feild p anely worthy scottis wrocht thair sa hardely schir iohne mortoun yat place deed twelf hundreth ony mair remeid thir mony left feild slane laif returnit toun agan rewit full sair euer yai furth couth foud amang yame full mony ane werkad wound oist agane ilk ane thair waird raid commandit wache na mair noyis maid bot restit still quhill bricht day dew agane began toun sailye new thus thay wrocht full greit worthynes assailyeit sair wit hardynes oistis vittall worth skant failyeit fast thus lay thay thair quhil diuers dayis war past land waistit meit nane win bot wist nocht folk within thay dred full sair thair awin vernysoun souerance prayit power toun speik wallace thay desyrit fast appeirit speirit quhat thay ast mair answerit said wald pay ransoun pa way deir na mair toun greit schame war suld yoldin tounis haldin le power ye may nocht wyn v lang thocht yat ye byde sall gif gold ye fra v ryde may gif battell durst king sen he left war ouir hie ane thing v without ordinance toun hald gouernance wallace answerit gold rek nocht battell hidder socht leuer haue battell ingland gold gude king arthur fand mont michell quhen giant slew nane ill na kin meane power toun bot gif king mak battell boun oist mony worthy man wallace rekkin better thay wrocht thocht best yit vther lak nocht sernit thank scotland euer mair manheid wit quhilk thay schewit thair haill counsall thus demit thame amang toun seige thay thocht lang nocht ane way wyn na slicht counsall fand best thay micht sum gold tak sen thay get na mair syne furth away thair
