withouttin wordis moir sa neuer na sutheroun befoir madame said richt welcum mot ye pleissit yow oisting se richt weill scho said freindschip haue neid god grant ye wald necessair speid suffer mon suppois lyke v ill bot traistis weill contrair ye sall remane lord man gang fra presence sall nocht tary lang erll vnto pauilloun yeid gude auyse deme mair deid counsall sone wallace gart call thame lordis said wait ye quhat ado thair cuming self he na plesance thairfoir man wirk ordinance wemen may contempning weir amang fuillis nocht thame forbeir say nocht thir quene trow bot gude scho mene exempill tak lang tyme passit runsy vaill tressoun planely wemen maid yat ganzelone brocht turky wyne forbeir couth thay nocht lang vse weir gart thame desyre thair quhilk brocht king charlis felloun lois ill flour france without redemptioun throw foull deid brocht confusioun command men thairfoir priuat wyse pane lyfe thay wirk nocht sic gyse nane speik yame bot wyse men greit vaill lordis ar sworne counsall charge thay al gudly thay mocht ordinance throw oist wrocht erll baith quene thay went ressauit hir fair brocht hir ane tent denner bownit al gudly thay seruit mony lyklie man gude purueyance quene hir brocht ane assay scho tuik gude hir thocht wallace persauit said haue na dreid nocht trow ladyis deid poysoun men ingland wyn quene answerit gif poysoun thairin ony thing quhilk brocht heir vpon self first sorrow ye sall se sone efter meit ane marschell gart absent bot lordis thay counsall went ladyis appeirit presence quene wallace askit quhat hir cuming micht mene peice scho said haue yow socht byrnand weir baill he mony brocht ye grant v peice deit tre wallace answerit madame may nocht ingland he done sa greit harmis v may nocht pa lichtly leif thus yes said quene cristin folk ar goddis saik sen desyre na mair aucht haue peice said deny perfite caus sall schew quhy ye seik na peice bot awin auaill quhen yat king scotland grippit haill na kin thing befoir fand wald nocht thoill richt blude land bot reft thair rent syne put thame self deid ransoun gold micht mak v na remeid fell fals weir sall self sene soberly answerit quene thir wrangis amendis war maist fair madame said ask na mair bot wald byde v battall god iudge kennis mater haill sic thing scho said war nocht gude think peice war best micht purchest wald ye grant peice trewis v tak throw ingland suld gar prayeris mak yow yame yat weir war loist wallace said quhair sic cumis throw boist prayer force quhair sa wrocht v helpis outher lytill nocht warly scho said thus wyse men he v kend ay efter weir peice finall end quhairfoir ye suld greit malice ceis end weir cheritie pei peice heuin blis lestandnes sall beseik lord hie grace command peice sen may na mair madame said prayer cum thair mendis ingland think yan haue quhat set yow thus weir sa god yow saue fra violent weir ye think nocht dwell madame said treuth sall yow tell efter dait alexanderis ring land thre yeir stuid desolat king keipit full weill concord gude stait throw twa yat clamit thair hapnit greit debait sa ernistfully accord thame nocht thay king thay askit thair ouir man slely slaid strenthis scotland kingrik syne tuik awin hand maid ane king aganis richteous law suld haue regioun aw contrair band war haill barnage scotland yit neuer thirlage greit iulius tribute tuik wynning scotland bot richt small fals king vnder collour mair throw band maid bruce air vndid king quhilk befoir maid throw scotland greit power yai raid bruce sen syne keipit na cunnand said wald nocht gang conqueis land vther men thus cace befell scotland throw demanit sell slew eldaris greit pietie se presoun syne lang tyme thay presonit quhill cassin deid thankit god send sum remeid vengit preuit micht feill kin deith syne haue dicht rage youth gart desyre ane wyfe rewit sair lyfe ane tratour knicht mercy gart hir de ane hessilrig bot despyte rang furth trauell weir pane quhill redemit part land agane counsall desyrit v ane trew quhilk maid scotland full graithly rew peice thay set ane subtill air xviij scoir deith thay hangit thair nobillis war worthy renoun coit armouris eldest regioun deith wethink venge micht woman al duilfully dicht mynd deith neuer slyde quhill god tak fra fals warld sa wyde sutheroun sen na pietie haif men weir neuer think saif bricht teiris pietie behald brist fra ene quhen taill tald quene weipit pietie wallace allace scho said wa worth wickit cace waryit tyme hessilrig borne mony worthy throw deith ar forlorne suld haue pane saikles sic ane sleu h ingland sen syne he bocht deir aneuch thocht scho bene ane quene ane prince madame said al god gif gude grace prince quene quhat stait sa thay hir tyme scho al deir wallace scho said talk ceis mendis heirof gude prayer pei grant said na mair richt nocht bot eiking cair quene fand weill langage na thing hir bet scho trowit gold micht ouirset thre thousand pund fynest gold sa reid scho gart brocht wallace steid madame said na sic tribute craif ane vther mendis wald ingland haif returne ra regioun agane fals b ude he eldaris slane gold rich ring ye get na peice desyre king quhen scho saw weill gold micht hir nocht releif sum part sport scho thocht preif wallace scho said ye war clepit lufe mair aboundantly maid prufe traisting thairfoir rancour slaik think ye suld sum thing saik richt wyselie maid answer quene madame said veritie war sene ye luifit aucht yow lufe agane thir wordis ar nathing bot vane speiche lufe subtill ye sutheroun ar ye v mok suppois get na mair tak ane lyking syne get na plesance sic lufe nathing auance londoun scho said yow sufferit blame counsall al lauch quhen cum hame sa may thay say wemen ar feirs thocht seik freindschip syne get richt nocht madame wait ye war hidder send ye trow haue bot lytill spend first gold ye ar riche wi ye wald v blind sen scottis ar sa ny syne plesand wordis yow ladyis fair quha suld dryfe byrdis ane snair ane quhissill pype freschest call madame yit ye may nocht tempt v greit part gude left amang kyn ingland al find aneuch wyn abaissit scho mak answer till deir schir scho said sen weir peice quhat yow lykis best lat hie wit gude counsall degest madame said sall ye vnderstand ressoun quhy mak na band yow ladyis na trewis bynd fals king wald sone heirefter fynd quhen saw tyme brek planely say grantit nocht thair till nane bot ladyis reprufe sall nocht god sittis abufe vpon wemen na weir begin yow feild na worschip win haill pais self sall tak peice weir quhat happin mak quene grantit answer sufficient sa laif plane present deliuerance thay held greit auaill stark aneuch schaw thair counsall wa quene hir trauell helpit nocht gold scho tuik yai hir brocht oist richt frely scho gaif euerie man lykit haif menstrallis heraldis scho gaif aboundantle beseikand thame hir freind thay wald quhen wallace saw fredome quene sadly said suith weill he bene sene wemen may tempt wysest he bene wrocht greit gentrice sall nocht yow assure oist sall na thing quhill tyme ye may send message fra king gif swa accord saik sall better heraldis al sall saifly cum ga fredome sall trubill na scho thankit grant mony syse ladyis vpon ane gudly wyse glaidly thay drink quene gude wallace hir ladyis al lordis place hir leif scho tuik outtin langer baid fyue myle nicht south ane nonry raid vpon morne londoun passit thay westmynster quhair counsall lay wallace answer scho gart schaw king neidis nocht heir mair reheirs thing greit commend scho wallace gaif befoir king presence laif trew scottis suld greitly appleis thocht inglismen thairof lytill eis worschip wit manheid gouernance fredome treuth key remembrance scho callit thair thair hie presence thocht contrair thame stude defence sa chiftane lyke scho sayis sene ingland trow he neuer bene wald ye gold gif realmis rent fra honour nocht turne intent assouerit ye ar quhill ye may message mak wyse lordis sum part reid yow tak purches peice withouttin wordis mair ingland may rew raid full sair heraldis al pa he leif oist thair sall na man thame greif thankit thay quene hir trauell king lordis war counsell hir answer king appleissit thre greit lordis thay ordanit pa thair counsall haill he fund best trewis tak elli thay get na rest ane herald went haist may auane vaill quhair scottis lay conduct haue till thay said thair counsall sone ane conduct send thame till agane past souerance king cheissit thay thre lordis thing kene cliffurd wardane haill bewmont wodstok men mekill vaill quhat thir thre wrocht ye laif suld stand yair till kingis self geuin thame thair sone thay war brocht speiking wallace wodstok schewit furth mony subtill cace wallace he hard thair sophysmis euerilk deill yit said think mene bot weill wrang ye hald doi v greit outrage housis part heritage peice plane mak thame knawin thame wyn sen thay ar awin roxburgh berwik yat ouris lang tyme he bene handis fals king wene ask heir al vertew band awin youg king wrang led fra scotlad sall thame haue withouttin wordis mair desyre lordis grantit thair richt thay haue consentit haill na kyn thing peice thay wald nocht faill young randall londoun lord lorne band erll buchane bot tender age efter grew ane man greit vassalage cumyng foullis gart delyuer al quhilk efter king robert full fals wallange fled ouir durst nocht byde yat mute picardy ask na bute bot wald erar haue fals knicht ane thousand fynest gold sa bricht bruce askit bot away befoir tyme calice mony ane day king edward preuit yat yai micht nocht get glocester vncle fet calice haill keiping wallace tyme gat nocht richteous king erll patrik al fra londoun thay send wallace gang weill befoir kend mater ane finall gouernance king edward gaif vp legeance tuik hald scotland euer mair full glaid hait wallace ressauit yair thay honourit richt reuerently lord scottis reioysit concord ane hundreth hors young lordis renou wallace come fred presoun vnder seill king edward yan gart send gif ouir mak ane finall end roxburgh berwik quhilk war mekill vaill scottis men boundis haill syne yeir trewis thay promeist yair band wallace said pa neir scotland ocht seillit thairfoir mak v boun agane besyde northallartoun quhair king edward first battell hecht began thair sall endit greit weill quene chargit message hir leif veyage ane day set quhen thay suld meit thair seill peice withouttin proces mair vpon morne oist mair auyse tranoyutit left thair big hicht syne marche agane rydis richt roxburgh thay cheissit ane place ane gude towr thair gart big schort space kingrik stude gude worschip eis nane sa greit durst nichtbour displeis ane end syue scotland bad suld wend wrait richt verray greit honour william wallace ane conquerour louit leid worschip wyse wicht thow verray help halding thy richt thow richt reskewar thy natiue land land thame sent glaid hartis atanis thay went vnto schip thay rowit haistely seymen wirkand full ernestly ankeris wand wyselie ather syde thair leidis kest waittit weill tyde leit saillis fall he thair cours anone ane gudly wynd richt airth come freikis foirstam reullit weill thair geir leidis lebuird ane lordly feir lynis laid luik thair passage sound ful saill yus fra scotland firth yai foud nane gold vther gude bot slayis drownis derfly flude gettis na grace thocht war king knicht sextene ye ir he done greit vnricht power sa strang he steir may nane eschaip yat cumis dangeir wald ye buird na buit begin lakest schip floit within may saill v doun vnto dulefull deid wallace said sen thow na remeid tell feir sall knaw quhat vse syne go luge law schip men said full weill ye may ken graith takynnis full cleirly men co armour sene mony steid battell bown rayment reid formest schip persewis v sa fast self nocht agast yow haill quhen yat thay cum yow neir without tary man ye stryke steir self enter first full hardely thir ar signis yat ye sall tak ane bar blew schynand scheild ane bend quhyte desyrand ay feild reid betakynis blude hardyment quhyte curage incressand intent blew beiris cristin man sadly answerit william wallace thocht cristin na cristin deid ga vnder loft ye lord god mot v speid baith schipmaister steirisman also baid gart thame go fyfcie men withouttin langer rest wallace gart ray thair armour prest aucht fourtie lufe buird laid thay law william craufurd caw said thow sum part schipman fair thow he bene vsit toun air pray tak doctrine weill luik thow stand still straitly tre quhen thay bid stryke seruice thow bane quhen warne lat doun saill agane cleland cousing cum tak steir hand heir waill neir sall stand god gyde schip say na mair barge began ane ful weirlyke fair self loft ane drawin sword bad yair steirisman lay endlang buird loud cryit stryke doggis ye sall de craufurd leit draw saill lytill capitane lap ful sone wald slynt wallace he sone gorget hynt ouir loft kest quhair yat stude quhill neis mouth ruschit turth blude ane forgit knyfe braithly braidit weir schippis lappit thame barge clippit bot thay nocht festnit fast craufurd drew saill schot thame past reuar cryit pieteous voce full cleir grace lyfe yat bocht v deir mercy cryit deit rude laser mend haue spilt mekill blude trespas wald mak sum remeid mony saikles haue gart put deid wallace wist weill thocht deith war brocht fra thame chaip na wyse micht nocht lyfe sum reskew micht mak ane better purpois syne sone tak al rewit lyfe bene ill latine toung richt men said wallace pei thair schot gun nocht eith ceis thay castand war awfull ather syde reid reuar commandit thame byde held vp ane gluif taikning trew men beheld weill senye knew left thair schot signe quhen yat yai saw greitest barge towart caw lat e weir thir ar freindis ane trow god werst houri ar gane askit wallace quhat schort auyse richt thus said till rochell wald ye gart thame saill mair man wyselie speirit quhat land art thow borne france said elderis beforne thair sum part heritage thocht feirs fortoun yus brocht ane rage wallace answerit come thow lyfe forsuith said bot throw ane suddand stryfe sa happinit kingis presence ouir recklesly ane greit offence ane worthy man gude kyn renoun throw deid put confusioun deid ane straik quhat neidis wordis mair mendis nocht thocht repent sair throw freind court chaipit place neuer sen syne couth get kingis grace feill kyn thay gart saik de fra tyme saw micht na better bot leif land behuifit neid vpon ane day burdeous yeid ane inglis schip sa gat ane niche sey laubour full ernestly v dicht assemblit mysdoaris vther within schort space multiplyit sa micht contrair power gang tyrannie thus haue rungin lang thir sextene yeiris haue bene se done greit harme thairfoir full wa saifit quhene gold greit ransoun bot slew drownit sey doun fauour folk sindrie land bot frenche men na freindschip fand thay gat na grace al far micht ring al sey cleipit ane king se weill fortoun went vin ust ane garris sair repent quha wald haue said samin day morne suld ane thus lichtly doun borne greit heithing men wald haue tane self thocht al haue matchit ony ane bot haue fund verray plane contrair heir gif ouir rubrie euer mair mysreull sall neuer armes beir bot gif honest vse weir haue tald part blis pane goddis saik sum kyndnes kyith agane hart brek bot wit quhat ye outrageously he rebutit weill weind leuand bene nane force strenth micht presoner tane except wallace he redemit scotland best callit day leuand hand weir war worschip waik warld trow he na maik wallace smylit said freind may weill scotland neid mony sic quhat thy name tell sa haue thow seill forsuith said thomas longueill weill bruik thow thus styntis stryfe schaip said thomas may nocht bot gude freindschip sall keip gart draw wyne ilk ane mery maid schippis rochell raid reid blasouis yai borne weir toun sone ane suddand feir reid reuar thay said yair quhilk throw strenth micht nane aganis stand sum schippis fled sum ye land he tane clariounis blew trumpetis mony ane quhen wallace saw pepill steir gaif command na schip suld neirar peir bot awin barge yame lykit pa richt wist thair quhat scottisman wallace bot weil yai thocht ane gudly honourit craft thay thay four dayis still wallace remanit thair thir men callit quhen boun fair thame commandit vpon coist byde quhill thame fred chance yat micht betyde beir yow euinly quhat gude euer ye spend leif awin quhill yow tythingis send gar sell thir schippis mak yow men pei war gude tyme wickitnes ceis capitane sall pa king throw help god sall warrand gart graith suit win man na man thair yat micht weill thomas ken lyklie manly countenance lyk scottis mekill gouernance saif toung scottis nane latine weill micht haue sufficit ane thus past thay haist thay may paris toun thay went vpon ane day tythingis war brocht wallace king sa greit desyre na kin thing tyme quhill sene wallace meit self waittit vpon cace ane garding quhair gart thame brocht presence manlyke feir thay socht twa fyftie atanis kneland doun salust roy maist renoun reullit speiche sa gudly auyse france couth nocht mair nurtour yame deuyse quene leif come hir effeir mekill scho hard wallace deid weir quhat neidis mair courtesy tell thay keipit weill scottis befell kingis fair dar mak na reheirs febill mynd trubillit sprite transuers riche seruice quhat neidis wordis mair micht nane fund bot preseut thair sone efter meit king perlour went gudly lordis thair wallace present commonit thay mony sindrie thing speik greit desyre king speirit weir gouernance answerit manly countenance euerie point al far feill latine toung richt naturally weill king consauit sone hie knawlage quhat weirmen vsit reif thair passage quhat mynd reid reuar meruell said leit wallace pa said ye ar sum thing blame ye micht haue send herald fra hame efter power bring yow throw se god thank yow schir thairof aneuch men may pa quhair thay find na perrall richt quhene may keip quhair nane assaill wallace said thairof meruell haif ane tyran regnis ire full cruelly vpon sey greit sorrow he wrocht micht get suld nocht borne land ane natiue man thairfoir v greitest harme doi thomas quoik changit countenance hard king euill deidis disauance wallace beheld fenyeit ane part forsuith said fand nane art profferit v ony sic vnkyndnes full glaid hart wallace ressauit yame yair rothwen ramsay renoun ane trew scot yat past sact iohnstoun thame warning maid yat psewart followit fast vpon wallace war thay sair agast toun ischit thair micht thre hundreth yat worthy war wicht blak irnesyde assemblit place wallange gane gude wallace knicht psewart he weill thair cuming sene ane fair plane feild cheisit thame betuene elleuin hundreth four scoir scottis men war fyue hundreth sextie thir bot ane plane feild tak wod gude wallace mak wist na wit thame cumand mair hardiment fra strenth pa bot quhen hard rothuen ramsay cry ouchtirhous blyith cheualry micht thay gold haue brocht ane kingis rent gude wallace micht nocht sa weill content array thay yeid ather syde cruell ire battell bowne byde worthyer men psewart semblit thair tyme edward neuer mair bot psewart saw number far power sone gart deuyde twa fecht caus knichtly thame kend iourney outher wyn end worthy scottis yat first amang yame baid full greit slauchter inglismen thay maid wod befoir preuit weill plane thay sonyeit neuer adeill curage grew thay war new begun schort rest thay fra rysing sone ram ay gude worthy rothuane throw thickest preis gane sloppis thay maid amang inglismen disseuerit thame twentie ten quhen speiris war gane swordis mettel inglismen thair cuming sauld full deir wallace worthynes hand feill sutheroun blude gart licht vpon ye land twa feildis togidder reillit schir iohne psewart mony nobill man help thair lord thre hundreth ane place stude thair besynes defendand mony awfull dynt quhill outwart feild tynt commounis part forest fled su cour seik thir men sa thame led scottis he sene sa mony ane rout psewart stand inueronit vpon sydis assailyeit wounder sair poleist plaitis poyntis peirsit bair sutheroun maid defence full cruelly occupyit nobill cheualry schir iohne ramsay wald thay yoldin bene wallace said nay wrang ye mene ransoun tak nocht begin sic ane wyse land ye may nocht win yone knicht auld enemie he bene sa fell v thame haue nocht sene sall de throw help goddis grace come pay ransoun place sutheroun saw wist planely de reskew nane suppois thay wald fle freschly thay faucht thay enterit new vpon syde part worthy thair haill power tu k plane purpois fle quha eird wallace gart la thame vpon formest followit micht erll amang laif licht deith yat vnhorssit war yat ayde efter hors full freschly thay ryde fyue hundreth large thay past daiswy toun sutheroun syde ground brocht doun scottis hors mony began tyre suppois thair self feirs ony fyre flearis left baith wod watteris hill tak plane speidfull thay thocht thame till greit battell away full fast thay raid ye strenthis thay thocht mak na baid n ir lochmabane ochti hous thay went besyde croichmad quhair feill sutheroun sche richt mony hors runin sa lang trauellit sair thay micht na farther gang schir iohne ye grahame vpon fuir set wallace al lychtit withouttin let thir twa fuit amang yair enemeis yeid nane hors micht fra yame pa speid inglismen sa cruelly thay socht quhome thay ouirtuik agane harmit v nocht wallace come ane part power new restit hors peirtly couth persew adame corry gude men greit vaill iohnstoun al dwelt eskdaill kirkpatrik cumpany haliday quhilk semblit sturdily quhair thay enterit ye sa ye sa sair deid ground feill flearis doun thay vair seuin scoir haill new cumin men deid south partie yame mekill dreid wallace hors vpon ane cuirsour wicht gude corty brocht sicht stuf chace new cheualry commandit grahame gude men thy togidder dyde follow thay micht thre capitanis yair full sone deith yai dicht restit hors sa wounder weill bair quh ouirtuik agane rais neuer mair raithly raid wrocht full mony wound thir thre capitanis stikkit ane stound durrisdeir ennoch teberris mure lord cu urdis eme away carlile fure quhilk befoir yat keipit lochmabane na landit man cha pit bot ane maxwell al carlauerok come ye sutheroun ganest way he nome chace sa wilfully thay ryde gat away come vpon syde besyde cokpule full feill fechting thay fand sum drownit sum slane vpon land quha chaipit ingland fled away wallace returnit na presoner tuik thay carlauerok nicht resting thay maid vpon morne dumfreis bly thly raid thair wallace cryit quha wald cum pei aganis sutheroun thair malice ceis trew scottis ordanit warysoun quha taltit grantit remissioun dumfreis wald na langer byde sutheroun fled f scotland ilk syde sey land without langer abaid castellis toun yan wallace chiftanis maid reullit land put gude rest trew keiperis quhilkis traistit best gude dowglas yow tald air keiper fra drumlanerik air becaus sutheroun sie thing wrocht wyfe wraith bot yat scho schew nocht vnder couert hir malice held perfyte ane serpent waitis hir tyme yat scho may byte dowglas oft scho wrocht full mekill cair leif quhill farther mair bot sutheroun men durst yan na castellis hald thay left scotland befoir yow tald saif ane mortoun ane capitane feirs sell held dundie wallace wald nocht dwell thidder past lappit quhen mortoun saw yat dout askit leif thair lyfis ga wallace denyis sayis beis nocht swa last capitane ingland yat heir gaif leif haill men pa thow sall forthink sic maistrie mak ingland sall exempill tak sic men weind fra thyne haue worne thow salbe hangit suppois thy king sworne gart command na scottis suld yame speik confermit seige said sall v wreik inglismen skill dundie skrymgeour maid thair constabill ane ballingair ingland thair past tay come quhitbie fair londoun send tald cace hyng mortoun sa vowit wallace befoir tyme edward power yeid weir france na dreid befoir trowit scotland win quhen thay warnit men ouirthrawin agane tuik ingland haistely left deid fiklit foly gascoun clamit heritage left thus hie barnage flanderis al thocht tak hand thir left come reif scotland quhe yat desyre micht haue na rest thocht mak plane conquest couetise rungin sa lang chiftanis maid yat thay suld nocht pa wrang gydis thay theis fra strenthis thame gy thay thocht na mair byde ieopardy plane battell thay micht wallace wyn trowit weir thay wald na mair begyn leif king makand ordinance purpois speik sum thing france inglismen guyan held weir frenche folk yai full mekill deir king counsall sone thair wittis kest get wallace thame thocht best guyan land inglismen thay schuip thay thus haist thay may thay traistit gif scotland war weill stad wallace wald cum thame promeist samyn herald befoir scotland thay commandit ordanit suld pa scotland without langer delay sluce al gudly may reddy schip past cais tayis mouth baid hauin tai quhair wallace ye sailye still ressauit herald gude thair writ red said thame wyse ane answer sone couth thame nocht deuyse honest iunis herald send wallace coist richt baldly spend quhill tyme saw vther materis yeid answer suld haue withouttin dreid land defend thow vndois throw thy fals cruell deid thow he tint twa yat worth far mair meid vpon day ane gude king found fyue millioun fynest gold sa round euer wrocht werk cunye bricht trow warld richtous king wilfully distroyis thyne awin ofspring bruce answerit thow deuyse wallace said nay thow leuis sic ane wyse thow wald mak edwardis yit leuer ye morne hangit hie yit sall say wald counsall geif ane lord thow micht lyking leif thyne awin scotland ring peice hald edward king fals king think neuer tak bot contrair power mak clame na thing tytill richt thocht micht reif sen god he lent micht fra thy crown regioun weir bot nocht sic charge vpon beir greit god wait best quhat weir tuik hand keip fre thow art ganestandand micht said lang tyme beforne curssit tyme thow scotland borne schamis thow nocht neuer yit gude thow regnegat deuorar thy blude vow god may thy maister ony feild thow sall far rather de sall ane turk thy fals cruell weir paganis v doi nocht sa mekill deir leuch bruce wallace ernistnes said thow seis thus standis cais day thow art power ouirset aganis yone king ouirhand thow may get wallace said ar mekill thing starker day incontrary yone king bigger quhair fair groundin syith wallace leit draw gude chiftane clenely ouir lap thame aw guid sword maid ane hiddeous woud left deid syne feird found rig bane greit ire ta cleuit coist richt cruelly twa thre formest syithis yi gude wallace ouir lap four slew yai saw sic thair hap ane man ay slew euerilk straik last fled first thair power laik wallace followis sone fyft ouirtais straik deith na farther gais syne sped sone vnto men agane thay knichtis brother slane fyftie sex derfly deith dicht except seuin men fled thair sicht fyue mawaris al wallace self met frenchemen sen syne na sic tryst set becaus thay brocht sic ane cace king hard tell weill chaipit wallace send sone syne prayit houshald leif gude saiftie weill saw thay inuy still self gart byde thy twa yeiris thair wallace myrth abaid still france mony gude iourney maid king pleisit gudly mane fra thocht suld nocht part agane lordis ladyis honourit reuerently wretchis schrewis ay inuy phow wallace slew twa campiounis cap twa campiounis yat time dwelt wt ye king greit despite wallace thing togidder yeid ay thir twa campiounis felloun force thrawart conditiounis richt greit despite thay spak ay scotland quhill ane day hapnit vpon hand wallace thay war leuit thame allane auenture ane hous stane thay vsit beir na wappinis hall thay trowit thairfoir ane mys yai micht fall thair commonnit thay scotland scornefully wallace said ye wrang v vtterly sen ar bund freindschip king v plesit thing scottismen he helpit realme fra dreid think ye suld gif gude word gude deid quhat may ye speik enemeis bot euill lichtlynes thay maid answer thair till dispytit thair langage al ye scottis thay said he euer yit bene fals wallace tuik ane face tene gude hand quhill neis mouth ene throw braith blaw buschit blude grouflingis groud smoit quhair stude tother hynt wallace steid weill weind fellow bene deid agane greif grippit sair quhill spreit failyeit yat micht na mair first freik rais smoit wallace fast baith deith brocht thame last vpon ane pillair thair harnis dang handis ye dur yame slang said quhat deuill mouit yone carllis lang tyme france wald haif lattin yame traist weill treuth thus war thay gane deid thocht frenche lykis yairof reid al ceis put ryme better quha richt luik tyme mony greit lord displeisit france bot ye gude king yat knew haill chance richt greit despite scotland spokin thay passit ouir quhill yat vpon ane day nane thame yat durst vndertak done wrang yairfoir battell mak phow wallace slew lyoun barrace cap iij royall roy ane hie worschip gaif conquerour honourit ouir ye laif ane fell lyoun yi king gart brocht within barrace greit harme yat wrocht tyrlisit irne na mair power gaif wodnes exceidit laif bot fair richt felloun deid strang strenth gart men feid keipit clos men bestiall court yair dwelt twa squyar greit vaill cousingis war ye capiouis twa quhilk befoir wallace hapnit sla ane band thay maid preuy conclusioun thair power wirk confusioun ony meane throw fraud subteltie efter yairfoir yai thocht nocht de deith schame sa yat yai micht bring vpon ane tyme thay went vnto king scot thay said ye sa weill fair mak seis nocht heir bot wald vndertak greit force put confusioun desyris fecht lyoun bad v ask yow battell strang ye grant leif barrace gang sadly agane thame answerit king sair forthinkis desyris sic thing bot nouther greif yit plesa ce deny wallace quhat desyris france went thay furth sone met wallace ane figurat taill thay tauld yat cace wallace thay said king desyris ye direnye battell sa cruell se chargis yow fecht lyoun wallace answerit haistie conclusioun sall quhat kingis power richt glaidly fulfill passit vnto king mair ane lord court quhen approchit thair vnwyselie speirit without prouisioun wallace dar ye ga fecht lyoun said ye sa king suffer self gif ye ocht better quhat ye mair thing admittit wallace suld vnto lyoun pa king chargit bring gude harnes said nay god scheild fra sic cais suld tak gif faucht ane man bot ane dog nocht armis haue nane bot singlil ga ane greit mantill hand ta ane gude sword tuik na mair abandoundly barrace enterit thair greit cheinyeis wrocht ye yet gin pullit quhen wallace thairin wod lyoun wallace quhair stude rampand brayit desyrit blude round pollis mantill rocht sa akwart bak yit wallace ta gude sword birneist steill body twa cuttit euerilk deill syne king raikit greit ire said loud desire wair ane scot lichtly vane thair doggis yat ye yit wald haue slane ga bring yame furth sen man doggis quell bidding quhill yat yow dwell ganis full weill graith scotland greiter deidis yair men he tane hand ane dog battell encheif yow france euer tak leif king persauit yat wallace greuit sa ernistly askit leif pa rewit mynd hapnit sa sa lewd ane deid lat vnderta knawand worschip ye greit nobilnes quhilk sprang yat tyme mony place hamely said suld displeis yow nocht ye desyrit bred neuer thocht faith aw crown france thocht neuer charge yow sic chance bot men vaill askit yow wallace answerit god mak ane vow lykit neuer sic battell vpon ane dog na worschip win king consauit falset wrocht squyaris baith presence brocht culd nocht deny quhen thay come befoir thair trespas thay tald withouttin moir king commandit yai suld done deid smoit thair heidis without ny remeid campiounis lo inuy caus e suddad deith wallace yame brocht throw cais squyaris al fra yair falsnes kend inuy yame brocht baith ane suddand end lordis behald inuy euill dragoun cruell fyre byrnis regioun nocht yat aboundis inuy sum mischeif bringis thame haistely forsaik inuy thow sall better speid heirof na farther reid bot mater befoir began sall declair al planely qvhen wallace saw thay inuy langer byde couth nocht yan planely better thocht scotland auenture tak outher leif de help awin far mair plesance thair byde welth france haill mynd manheid curage planely set wyn bondage scotland agane fra pane mekill schoir vowit suld elli de thairfoir king he sene gude wallace set letter gaif withouttin let quhilk lait fra scotland send wallace saw weill yair harmis kend first writ thairto accordiall thame supple thocht wald nocht faill quhairof suld heirof lang proces mak wallace france ane gudly leif tak king he sene wald nocht elli chalmer went behald micht nocht greit langour quhen wallace remufe king keipit kyndnes ay lufe iowellis gold worschip saif bad thame gif al mekill wald haif lordis ladyis weipit wounder fast quhen wallace thair sa tuik leif past na man tuik bot quham thidder brocht agane gude longoueill furth socht pane blis yat gude knicht left neuer cace befell quhill deith maid yame disseuer towart sluce gudlie feir past ane veschell gat maid se aucht schipmen feyit gudly wage yame gaif scotland fure firth tay thay haif phow wallace come scotland agane battell elchok park cap iiij vpon nicht wallace land he tane ernis mouth elchok gane gart schip couert saill away sa sicht thay war day elchok dwelt ane wallace cousing deir craufurd hecht ye hous quhe yai come neir bak syde wallace ane wyndo fand callit syne craufurd come hand fra tyme wist gude wallace barn ordanit yame ane place ane mow corne biggit thame closit weill nane micht persaif thair bot ane place quhair meit yame brocht bedding al gudly mocht ane dern hoill furth north syde thay vnto watter quhair wallace glaid four dayis fyue rest yai soiornit thair quhill meit gane craufurd bownit mair sact iohnstoun yair purueyance inglismen thocht tuik mair aboundantly wount ony tyme befoir thay haue tane put presoun oir quhat gaistis tell thay maid requeist said bot ane kirking feist yit thay presumit cuming wallace knawledge get yai set ane subtell race thay leit pa thing bocht syne efter sone haist thay mocht harnes yeid power toun aucht hudreth men wt buttellar maid yame boun followit dreich quhill yat yi man come hame wallace saw said seruit blame sleiping ane fell visioun tald till inglismen thow suld haue sald craufurd said bene torment sair inglismen dispair thairfoir ryse vp sone sum succour se dreid full sair thay set wachis worthy scottis yai graith yame guid weid thair wappinis tuik syne hous thay yeid thus suddandly thir feill sutheroun yai saw thay war fecht agane thame aw kenely come youg buttellar ye knicht wallace said ane plane land nocht richt bot elchok park neir heir besyde first sail ye think thair abyde nyntene thay war craufurd gude wil twentie man number fulfill park thay tuik wallace ane place he sene ot greit holing yat grew baith heich grene thortour treis ane maner strenth maid war wyn thay thocht gar feill de wod thick bot lytill breid lenth yai meit yai thocht hald strenth inglismen past craufurdis place fand barn ludgeing wallace craufurdis wyfe handis thay haue tane askit hir quhat way scottis gane richt weill thay trowit wallace suld yair fra france tay cumit throw se scho wald nocht tell boist yit rewaird tha buttellar said ouir lag thow he bene spaird thair grew matalent ire gart thame big ane braid byrnand fire sutheroun swore yairin scho suld brynt wallace said scho sall nocht end greit sin war yone faikles wicht sla scho suld end faith yair sall de left strenth plane feild ta loud cryit said lo heir thy fa thinkis thow schame tormet ane wyfe cum first mak end stryfe fra buttellar feild gude wallace sene auld malice woxe neir wod tene vpon ye scottis thay schuip greit mane gude wallace sone strenth tuik agane ane feill bikker inglismen began assailyeit sair mony cruell man bot yai within war nobill defence maid greit debait force violence entrie fyftene thay put deid laif remouit fra steid ye array agane sailye new wallace beheld quhilk weill weir knew fellowis said agane place thay nocht faill bot thus standis cace yone knicht thinkis deuyde men seir placis suith ye sall weill ken agane v preif may v behouis sum vther way se contrair thair micht ane gude defence mak longoueill thow sall sex tak william eme al mony sall yow ga lyue haue na knicht buttellar partit men thre wallace vesyit quhair buttellar schuip thidder yan past entrie weir quhilk syde thay assailye greit feir wallace leit part entrie begin bot nane yeid scottis come seuin formest frount first yeid wallace fyue men douchtie deid ilk ane slew ane wallace gart twa de buttellar neist said yi nocht abak drew leit curage slaik worthy scottis preuit weill scotland saik gude longoueill counter dang starkest man hand hynt harnis dang ane tre sword gat sone efter rais campioun lyke amang four gais euer ane man gart de ane dynt quhe twa deid ye tother thre wald stynt maid thame fle bot na bute yat he warld hald help mony felloun thrang glaid cheir thus vnto erne gang baith roistit flesche yair al breid cheis succour yame yat point lei deillis four men fyftie quhilk befoir fastit ouir dayis scoir deith thay bair yit inglismen cruell kene full derfly faucht quhair douchtie deid sene fra west yet drew scottis haill fechtaris quhen yai saw nocht auaill bot agane full fast thay thame speid knicht dundas preuit douchtie deid ouir neir yet full bandounly baid ane gude sword full greit maistrie maid nocht wittand weill fellowis fra yet sutheroun ta vnto erll thay led haistelie quhen saw said suld nocht de slay ane may v lytill remeid send furth wallace steid vnto north battellis he brocht quhill saw wist richt nocht send erll thankit largelie hecht quyte quhen sic caus micht se bot yit yairfoir souerance wald nocht grant thocht thay war yoldin cum recryant gold gude wald na tribute tak ane greit assault began mak erll fyfe dwelt vnder trewis lang king edward thocht wrang wallace sa seigand sanct iohnstoun bot gif come richt help crown inglismen wald nocht keip band come sone gude men land iohne wallange yan schiref fyfe wallace past starkit stryfe erll cumin gude trew nobill blude ye auld thane quhilk tyme gude sanct iohnstoun yai gang felloun sault hiddeous schairp strang full feill faggaldis dyke thay cast haddir hay wound flaikis fast treis eird ane greit passage yai maid ouir wallis thay yeid battell braid sutheroun maid greit defence agane quhil wallis thair ane thousand slane wallace yeid rayit battell richt sutheroun men derfly deith yai dicht saif erll wallace herald send gude iop self quhilk befoir kend dundas saik said suld nocht de wallace self thus ordanit ane small haiknay gart tak siluer gold coistis mak set cloik ane takin se ane lyoun wa e suld conduct conuoyit furth na man wemen barnis wallace gart freith yame syne cryit trew scottis thair awin pleneist ye lad quhilk lang bene ouirthrawin wallace past south land se edward bruce tyme richt worthie yeir befoir ireland bene thair cruell men kene fyftie feir motheris kin kirkcudbricht galloway enterit thay fyftie vincust nyne scoir syne past withouttin tary moir wigtoun sone castell he tane sutheroun fled left allane wallace met trew men reuerentlie lochmabane went cheualrie thay maid edward baith lord leidar yair conditioun wallace maid mair bot ane schort tyme byde robert king gif come nocht regioun ring edward suld ressaif crown faill hecht wallace barnage haill lochmabane prince edward leyndit still wallace past cumnok gude blak bog quhair wount vpon steid ane royall hous held inglis wardanis londoun past mair tauld king thair greit mysfair wallace scotland fra thame reduce ressauit edward bruce commounis swore yai suld cum neuer mair vpon scotland wallace leuand wair edward wrait menteith priualy prayit haist tyme passit promeis ye quhilk yat bundin schir iohne menteith wit he fundin suld best purpois fulfill sister sone haist callit till ordanit dwelling wallace ane aith agane gart mak cace quhat tyme wist wallace quyet draw suld warne quhat auenture micht faw man grantit sic thing suld done wallace thus seruice sone bot tressoun wallace lytill thocht lauborous mynd vther materis wrocht thus wallace thryis he maid scotland fre desyrit lestand peice weir sum part irk purpoisit serue god kirk leif vnder richteous king desyrit atouir eirdly thing phow wallace betraisit schir iohn menteith ingland martyrit thair cap v herald iop ingland sone send wrait bruce richt hartly comend beseikand cum tak crown nane suld ganestand clerk burges barrou herald past quhen bruce saw credance thairof tuik ane perfyte greit plesance awin hand agane wrait wallace thankit lawtie kyndnes beseikand mater conceill behouit ingland steill lang befoir keipit ragment quhilk cumyng byde parliament londoun gif thay accuse cum fra thame suld mak sum excuse prayit wallace glasgow mure waik nixt first nicht iulij saik bad suld bot quyet micht bring cheualrie wallace blyith quhen wryting saw houshald sone gart glasgow draw moneth thair ordanit thame byde keirly tuik ilk nicht ryde young man yat menteith send wist nane bot yir quhat way yat wallace wend quhilk gart warne eme xviij nicht sextie full sone schir iohn meteith gart dicht awin kyn allya borne tressoun gart yame sworne fra dunbertane yai sped thame haistely neir glasgow kirk thay buskit yame priuely wallace past furth quhair yat ye tryst set ane spy thay maid followit let robert railstoun neir way besyde bot ane hous quhair wallace vsit byde woik fuit quhill passit mydnicht keirly ane eip yame dicht thay bad man suld walk part walkin wallace come men fra ony art quhen thay sleipit yi tratour tuik gude h id met eme bad haue na dreid sleip bot ane man ye may haue ony craft without hous thair wappinnis laid yame fra weill thay wist gat wallace ane tha feit ransoun suld sauld thus semblit thay febill hauld tratour wa fra wallace stall baith knyfe sword bow arrowis efter mydnicht handis thay haue tane slomerit sleip na man bot ane keirly thay tuik led fra place deith withouttin langer space thay thocht bynd wallace strethis strag fuit gat thay fell tratouris amang grippit bot na wappin fand vpon ane sill saw besyde stand bak ane bristit thrang ane vther harnis dang al mony handis couth lay force hynt haue away bot power ane fuit micht nocht leid hous quhill yai war deid schir iohne saw weill force couth war tane erar thocht de menteith bad ceis thus spak wallace syne schew furth ane full richt subtell cace ye haue sa lang heir vsit yow allane quhill wit thairof ingland gane thairfoir heir sober curage inglismen ane full greit barnage ar semblit heir set hous ye force na wayis may wyn suppois ye strenth gude hector amang oist ye may nocht lang indure thay yow tak haist deith dicht haue spokin lord cliffurd knicht thair chiftane weill menit lyfe thay ask na mair bot quyte stryfe dunbartane ye sall pa furth awin hous ye may saiftie sutheroun sic vse menteith lang thay wallace trowit sum part wald say menteith said schir lo wappinis na e haif come traist lyfe gif micht saif wallace trowit weill gossop thryis wald nocht na maner wyis betrais scotland sa wyde ane aith askit tyde thair wantit wit quhat suld aithis moi forsworne lang tyme befoir aith maid wallace come richt fraudfully thus schewit till gossop said presoner yai mon yow se yan throw force yai tak yow fra ane courche slicht vpon handis yai laid vnder syne sicker cordis thay braid baith schairp teuch fast togidder drew allace bruce micht fair bynding rew quhilk maid scotland sone brokin vpon cace cumyngis deith lois gude wallace thay led furth feir amang thame aw keirly myst na sutheroun saw wist weill betraissit towart south quhen yai pa yit thay said trenth suld nochc de king edward wald keip gude saiftie honour weir wrocht sair bandis sa trublit thocht credence thairto forsuith couth nocht geif wist full weill thay wald nocht lat leif ane fals foull cais yat menteith he sald quhen wyse gude wallace cald sum men sayis saif lord thay leid maid fals record fawkirk gude stewart slane chronicklis reheirsis plane magdalene day xviij yeir befoir cumyngis deith thairfoir witnessis moir restoun wallace tressonabilly thus falsly stollin fra gude cheualry glasgow lay wist nocht thing thus loist byding king south thay led ay haldand waist land deliuerit haist ouir sulway sand lord cliffurd wallange tuik thair carleill toun full fast thay fair presoun set ane greit dolour hous efter thay callit wallace tour sum men syne said yat knew weill ye cace berwik toun deith thay put wallace contrair knawin opinioun scottismen berwik toun scotland fre vntill yat soullis gaif lord cumyng ingland laif ane vther point tratouris durst nocht pa sauld sa quhair scottismen maister thrid point ye commounis ingland quhat thay deny thay nocht vnderstand thing done witnes may na credence gif farther yai may se se de edward mair desyre lord haill empyre caus thay keipit sa lang quhill ye commounis micht vnto londoun gag pallace scotland quhome sall thow coplene allace fra pane quha sall refrene allace thy help fastly brocht ground best chiftane braith bandis bund allace thow he loissit thy gyde licht allace quha sall defend thy richt allace thy pane approchit wounder neir sorrow sone thow man left steir thy gracious gyde thy greitest gouernour allace ouir neir cum thy fatall hour allace quha sall beit thy baill allace quhen sall harmis thow haill quha sall defend quha sall mak fre allace weir quha sall thy helper quha sall keip quha sall redeme allace quha sall saxonis fra fleme na mair bot beseik god grace restoir haist welth peice sen gude wallace may succour na mair lois incressis mekill cair men glasgow still lay quhat sorrow rais quhen thay missit away cruell pane wofull complening thairof tell war ouir heuy thing lat speik thairof na mair lytill reheirs ouir mekill cair principally quhair redemptioun nane helpis nocht tell thair pieteous mane deith yairof yit remembrance lat slaik sorrow ballance bot longoueill lochmabane pa yair hecht quhair gud prince edward scotland suld pa neuer mair lois wallace socht hart sa air realme france vowit neuer se bot avenge wallace elli yairfoir de thair remanit quhill cuming king bruce weir yi guid knicht furth ring remembrance syne brucis buik secund quhe yai sanct iohnstou tuik followit king wynning toun bruce thairfoir gaif full greit guardoun charteris landis ye gude king gaif charteris sen syne kyn laif quhairto suld far story wend b buik mak ane finall end robert bruce come hame thrid day scotland efter wallace away lochmabane quhair fand gude edwart quhairof greitly reioysit hart bot fra wist wallace away led sa mekill baill breist bred neir wit worthit weid edward full sone yan brother yeid ane suddand chance wa fra weill gude edward sayis yi helpis nocht adeill lat murning may na remeid ye haue tynt ye suld reuenge deid bot caus tuik weir hand defence thryis he fred scotland quhilk tynt fra v kyn war nocht wallace neuer enterit myrrour lawtie manheid weir best euer sall power leid lykit haue tane crown wald nane let yat regioun nocht bene ye suld na entres realme tressoun falsnes sall ye se tratour sald fra yow thinkis dunbartane hald sum comfort tak lat slaik sorrow king chargit edward vpon morrow redres tak wrang yat wrocht dalswyntoun ordanit pa men armis gif yai fand cumyng thair put deith na dreid thay suld spair thay fand nocht king efter ew drumfreis quhai witnes anew hapnit wrang ouir greit haist ane king wirk law may skaith mekill thing neid nocht heir na farther schaw done knawin yow aw bot young dowglas first king ca pa weir yat wicht worthy ye king he tane ye croun heir ma bot schort mentioun lord sou gaif berwik toun away efter sone tynt galloway iohne lorne agane richt king rais ather syde bruce mony fais bald breichen contrair king couth ryde richt weir byde north geuin fra gude king quhilk maid lang panefull weir ring bot trew iames ye gude dowglas brucis richt ba weill mony place vnder king best chiftane bot wallace set ane chiftane allane thairfoir na comparisoun ane man saif reuerence crown bot sa mony dowglas he bene gude thing neuer scotland sene comparisounis nocht weill declair brucis buik speik na mair maister iohne barbour quhilk ane worthy clerk said bruce amang vther week mater prolixt maist purpois breifly haist gude wallace set amang fais londoun cliffurd wallange gais quhair king edward richt fane ye fang thay haue set richt ane presoun strang wallace end self wald leif dreid say werst bot richteousnes leid fynd lyfe sa verray trew fatall hour nocht fenye menteith sauld yat ouir weill knawin feill kyn scotland yan sawin chargit byde vnder greit iudgement king robert actit parliament thairof mak na langer continewance bot wallace end warld displesance thairfoir ceis puttis nocht ryme scotland may thank blyssit happy tyme borne principall pointis twa first farther ga scotland fred brocht fra thirllage heuin he herberage preuit gude experiance wyse clerkis he yit remembrance pbecaus mair part thir thingis followand altogidder superstitious agreabill ye treuth goddis word haue thocht expedient admonische gude reidar albeit haue insert yame efter forme copie yit notwithstanding na thing le allow appru e tham ony treuth bot rather ane part haue retenit thame still schaw blyndnes errour tyme quhairin wer wer enforcit beleif sic vaniteis lei yat may steirit vp gif thankis eternall god he oppinnit thair eyis deliuerit yame ignorance yat yai may cleirly discerne betuix licht mirknes richt wrang vther part satisfie appetytis mony culd nocht esely permit ony thing tane away alterit wark quhair haue borne thame alterand almaist na thing heirin lest thay suld iudge v rasche haistie thairof libertie plesure ane monk bury abbay tyme ane richt religious man ane youg al ordour stude quhilk knew lyfe clene perfyte gude father monk vesyit seiknes warld suld pa cais brother saw spreit lyklie pa ane band richt ernestly couth cum agane schaw meid suld ask god gude deid grantit power preif cum agane gif god wald gif leif spreit changit yi warldis pane tyme come monk agane sic thing he bene voce sicht quhair appeirit yair schynit mekill licht lyke lanternis illuminit sa cleir warldly licht thairto micht na peir ane voce said thus god he grantit grace sall keip promeis place monk blyith clene figure fair bot ane fyre brand foirheid bair yat thocht mislydst laif quhair art thow spreit answer sa god saif purgatory lang sall thow thair bot half ane hour cum lytill mair purgatory lat weill wit ony place quhair god commit ane houri space yair iudgit passis suppois speik quhy he thow laif sa haill science thocht maist vaill quha prydis yairin yair laubour waist science cumis bot haly gaist efter thy hour quhatis thy passage euin quhen tyme cumis said lest heuin quhat tyme pray yow declair twa ar lyfe man befoir thair quhilk twa ar thay veritie ken first he bene ane greit slayer men yai keip martyr londoun toun wednisday befoir king commoun nane lyfe he sa mony slane brother said taill bot vane slauchter god abhominabill said spreit forsuith na fabill wallace defender scotland richteous weir tuik vpon hand thair richteousnes luiffit ouir laif thairfoir heuyn sall honour haif syne ane pure preist mekill commend tuik thank quhat thing god send godlynes gude deuotioun heuin sall haue lest warysoun thrid grantit throw goddis grace brother said tell place thay bot deme outher dreme raif said spreit witnes yow sall haif bellis sall ring ocht ye may quhen thay slay half ane hour day sa thay ye monk wist quhat yai throw braid bertane ye word yairof scailli spreit tuik leif goddis wallace end heir greit pietie wald nocht put men greit dolour bot lichtly pa ouir fatall hour wednisday yi fals sutheroun furth brocht martyr thay befoir wrocht wallace martyrit ye suith yow tell wer oswald edmond edward panis tell men armis led ane full greit rout ane bald spreit wallace blent ane preist askit deit tre king edward commandit clergie said charge pane lois lyfe nane sa bold yone tyran schryfe he rung lang incontrair hienes ane blissit bischop sone present place canterbery richteous lord aganis king maid richt record said self sall heir confessioun gif haue micht incontrair thy crown thow throw force sall stop fra thing vow god quhilk richteous king ingland sall interdyte mak knawin thow art ane heretyke sacrament kirk sall geif syne tak thy chois sterf lat leif war mair vaill worschip thy crown keip sic ane lyfe thy bandoun land gude yat thow he bot couetise ye ay fra honour dre thow he thy lyfe rung wrangous deid sall sene thy seid king gaif charge thay suld bischop ta bot wyse lordis counsallit lat ga wyse men said yat desyre richt wallace raikit thair sicht sadly hard confessioun end humbly god spreit commend lawly seruit hartly deuotioun vpon kneis said ane orisoun leif tuik westmynster raid cleuch men yai buir wallace baid vnto ane place martyrdome tak deith na furthering mak fra first nicht tane scotland thay keipit samin band na thing he done gude bot inglismen seruit cairfull fude warldly lyfe desyris sustenance thocht gat incontrair plesance thay threttie dayis bandis yai durst flaik quhill bund ane scamyll aik irne cheinyeis war baith stark kene ane clerk thay set heir quhat wald mene thow scot said yat sa greit wrang he done thy fatall hour thow seis approchis sone thow suld mynd remember thy mysdeid clerkis may quhen yai yair psalmes reid cristin saullis yat makis thame pray thair number yow may ane thay thow seis force thow man deceis wallace said thy round reheirs thow he na charge suppois done mys yone blissit bischop he hecht sall haue blys trow weill god sall admit thy simulate wordis sall conscience smit comfort haue way suld gang maist pane feill byde heir sa lang said clerk king oft send till thow micht haue scotland thy hald ceissit thy stryfe sa ane lord rungin furth thy lyfe wallace said thow speikis michty thing lestit gottin richteous king fra worthy bruce ressauit crown thocht haif maid ingland bandoun vtterly suld haue bene quhat pleisit saif thy king spill weill said clerk se thow repentis nocht wickitnes thow he ane felloun thocht nane warld he sa mony lane thairfoir ask think thow suld bane grace king syne barnage wallace smylit ane lytill langage grant said sum inglismen slew querrell thocht nocht half anew muifit na weir bot wyn awin baith god ye richt full weill he knawin thy frustrat wordis doi nocht bot tyris command goddis name lat ane schiref gart clerk sone fra pa richt thay durst grantit quhat wald ane psalter buik wallace euer fra chyldheid wald nocht seuer better trowit veyage speid bot dispuilyeit weid grace askit lord cliffurd knicht lat haue psalter buik sicht gart ane preist oppin befoir hald quhill thay done quhat yat yai wald steidfast red ocht thay thair feill sutheroun said wallace feld na sair gude deuotioun sa beginning continewit yair swa ending quhill speiche spreit atanis fair lestand blys trow euer mair nocht tell deuydit fyue partis ordanit pa yit spreit thus lyklines weill wallace lyfe quha he ane better eill may schew furth mair writ eloquence he done diligence efter prose geuin fra latine buik quhilk maister blair tyme vnder tuik fair latine compylit ane end gude witnes mair commend bischop sinklair lord dunkell gat buik confirmit sell verray treuth thairof na dreid self hard greit part wallace deid purpois haue send rome father kirk yairin gif dome bot maister blair al schir thomas gray efter wallace thay leuit mony ane day thir twa knew best gude schir williamis deid fra sextene yeir quhill nyne twentie yeid fourtie fyue wallace age cald tyme yat sutheroun sald thocht mater nocht plesance suithfast deid worthy auance worthy men reidis rurall dyte blame nocht buik thocht imperfyte suld haue thank sen na trauell spaird trauell na man hecht rewaird na charge king vther lord greit harme thocht gude deid suld smord haue said heir neir proces gais fenyeit nocht freindis yit fais coistis heirof na man bund sentence na le bot al mekill reheirsit nocht sa worthely nobill wallace wrocht bot ane point grant said ane mi thir twa knichtis suld blamit knicht wallace cragy richteous lord lyddaill al gart mak wrang record allartoun mure ye crown tuik ane day get battell myne author say thir twa gart say ane vther wyse maister blair part suppryse go nobill buik fulfillit sentence suppois thow barrane eloquence go worthy buik fulfillit worthy deid bot help langage thow he neid quhen
